barhiṣadaḥ pitaraḥ vividhāḥ punar menā ca dhāraṇī ca eva yābhyām dhatam idam jagat agniṣvāttāḥ tu ye proktāḥ teṣām menā tu mānasī dhāraṇī mānasī ca eva kanyā barhiṣadām smṛtā meroḥ tām dhāraṇīm nāma patnī artham vā sṛjan ghubhām pitaraḥ te barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ ye soma pāyinaḥ agniṣvāttāḥ tu tām menā patnī himavate daduḥ menā himavataḥ patnī mainākam sā vyajāyata gaṅgām saridvarām ca eva patnī yā lavaṇodadheḥ mainākasya ā tmajaḥ kraucaḥ kraiñcadvīpaḥ yatas smṛtaḥ mandaram suṣuve putram tisraḥ kanyāḥ ca viśrutāḥ velām ca niyatim ca eva tṛtīyām ca āyatim viduḥ dhātuḥ ca eva āyatiḥ patnī vidhātuḥ niyatiḥ smṛtā svāyam bhuveṃ'tare pūrvam yayoḥ vai kīrttitāḥ prajāḥ suṣuve sāgarāt velā kanyām ekām aninditām savarṇām nāma sāmudrīm patnīm prācīnabarhiṣaḥ savarṇāyām sutāḥ jātāḥ daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ teṣām svāyaṃbhuvaḥ dakṣaḥ putra tvam jagmi vān prabhuḥ trayaṃbakasya abhiśāpena cākṣuṣasya ātare manoḥ etat śutvā tatas sūtam apṛcchat śāṃśapāyaniḥ cākṣuṣasya antare pūrvam tat naḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām iti uktaḥ kathayāmāsa sūtaḥ dakṣa āśrayām kathām śāṃśapāyanim āmantrya tryaṃbakāt śāpa kāraṇam sūtaḥ uvāca dakṣasya āsan sutāḥ hi aṣṭau kanyāḥ yāḥ kīrttitāḥ mayā svebhyaḥ gṛhebhyaḥ ānāyya tāḥ pitā abhyarcayat gṛhe tatas tu abhyarcitāḥ sarvāḥ nyavasan tāḥ pituḥ gṛhe tāsām jyeṣṭhā satī nāma patnī yā tryaṃbakasya vai na ajuhāva ātmajām tām vai dakṣaḥ rudram abhidviṣan akarot saṃnatim dakṣe na kadācid maheśvaraḥ jāmātā śvaśure tasmin svabhāvāt tejasi sthitaḥ tatas jñātvā satī sarvāḥ nyavasan tāḥ pituḥ gṛhe jagāma sā api anāhūtā satī tatsva pituḥ gṛham tābhyaḥ hīnām pitā cakre satyāḥ pūjām a saṃmatām tatas abravīt sā pitaram devī krodhāt amarṣitā yavīyasībhyaḥ pi adhamām pūjām kṛtvā mama prabho a satkṛtya pitar mām tvam kṛtavān asi garhitam aham jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca tvam mām satkartum arha si evam uktaḥ abravīt enām dakṣaḥ saṃrakta locanaḥ tvattaḥ śreṣṭhau ariṣṭhāḥ ca pūjyāḥ bālāḥ sutāḥ mama tāsām ca eva tu bhartāraḥ ste me bahu mātāḥ sati brahmiṣṭhāḥ su tapaskāḥ ca mahā yogāḥ su dhārmikāḥ guṇaiḥ ca eva adhikāḥ ślāghyāḥ sarve te tryaṃbakāt sati vasiṣṭhaḥ atriḥ pulastyaḥ ca hi aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ bhṛguḥ marīciḥ ca tathā śraiṣṭhāḥ jāmātaraḥ mama yasmāt mām sparddhate śarvaḥ sadā ca eva avamanyate tena tvām na vibhūṣomi pratikūlaḥ hi me bhavaḥ iti uktavān tadā dakṣaḥ saṃpramūḍhena cetasā śāpa artham ātmanaḥ ca eva ye ca uktāḥ parama ṛṣayaḥ vāc manaḥ karmabhiḥ yasmāt aduṣṭām mām vigarhase tasmāt tyajāmi aham imam deham tāta tava ātmajam tatas tena avamānena satī duḥkhāt amarṣitā tatra api aham asaṃbhūtā saṃbhūtā dhārmikāt api tatra eva atha samāsīnā yuktā ātmānam samādadhe dhārayāmāsa ca āgneyīm dhāraṇām manasā ātmanaḥ tatas ātma samutthaḥ asyāḥ vāyunā samudīritaḥ tat upaśrutya nidhanam satyāḥ devaḥ atha śūlabhṛt saṃvādam ca tayoḥ buddhāḥ yāthātathyena śaṅkaraḥ dakṣasya ca ṛṣīṇām ca cukopa bhagavān prabhuḥ sarveṣām eva lokānām bhūrlokaḥ tu ādiḥ ucyate tam sadā dhārayiṣyāmi nideśāt parameṣṭhinaḥ asyām kṣitau dhṛtāḥ lokāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti bhāsvarāḥ tān aham dhārayā mī iha satatam ca tad ājñayā cāturvarṇyam hi devānām te ca api ekatra bhuñjate yasmāt avamatā dakṣa mad kṛte anāgasā satī praśastāḥ ca itarāḥ sarvāḥ sva sutāḥ bhartṛbhiḥ saha hute vai brahmaṇā śukre cākṣuṣasya ātare manoḥ abhivyāhṛtya sarvān tān dakṣam ca eva aśapat punar bhavitā mānuṣaḥ rājā cākṣuṣasya tvam anvaye prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraḥ ca eva prace tasām dakṣaḥ eva iha nāmnā tu māriṣāyām janiṣyasi kanyāyām śākhinām tvam vai prāpte vaivasvateṃ'tare yasmāt tvam mad kṛte aniṣṭam ṛṣīṇām kṛtavān asi tasmāt sārddham suraiḥ yajñe na tvām yakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ tatas abhivyāhṛtaḥ dakṣaḥ rudreṇa amita tejasā svāyaṃbhuvīm tanum tyaktvā utpannaḥ mānuṣeṣu iha jñātvā gṛhapatiḥ dakṣaḥ yajñānām mīśvaram prabhum menāyām tām umām devīm janayāmāsa śailarāj yā tu devī satī pūrvam āsīt paścāt umā bhavat sadā patnī bhavasya eṣā na tayā mucyate bhavaḥ marīcam kaśyapam devī yathā aditiḥ anuvratā yathā nārāyaṇam śrīḥ ca maghavatam śacī yathā viṣṇum kīrtiḥ ruṣā mūryam vasiṣṭham ca api arundhatī āvartamānāḥ kalpeṣu jāyante taiḥ punar saha evam prācetasaḥ dakṣaḥ jajñe vai cākṣuṣeṃ'tare daśabhyaḥ tu pracetobhyaḥ māriṣāyām punar nṛpaḥ jajñe tadā abhiśāpena dvitīyaḥ iti naḥ śrutam bhṛgu ādayaḥ ca ye sapta jajñire ca mahā ṛṣayaḥ iti eṣaḥ anuśayaḥ hi āsīt tayoḥ jāti antara anugaḥ tasmāt na anuśayaḥ kāryaḥ vaireṣu iha kadācana khyātim na muñcate jantuḥ tat na kāryam vipaścitā iti eṣā samanukrāntā kathā pāpa pramocanī yā dakṣam adhikṛtya iha tvayā pūrvam pracauditā pitṛ vaṃśa prasaṃgena kathā hi eṣā prakīrttitā pitṝṇām ānupūrvyeṇa devān vakṣyāmi atas param tretā yuga mukhe pūrvam āsan svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare devāyāmāḥ iti khyātāḥ pūrvam ye yajña sūnavaḥ prathitāḥ brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ aja tvāt ajitāḥ tu te putrāḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya ete śaktāḥ nāma tu mānasāḥ teṣām yatas gaṇāḥ hi ete devānām tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ vāyavyaḥ saṃyamaḥ ca eva yāmāḥ dvādaśa kīrttitāḥ asamaḥ ca ugradṛṣṭiḥ ca sunayaḥ atha śuciśravāḥ canimā viśvadevā ca javiṣṭhaḥ mitavān api śrutiḥ gṛṇānaḥ atha bṛhat śukrāḥ dvādaśa kīrttitāḥ āsan svāyaṃbhuvasya ete ca antare soma pāyinaḥ dīptimantaḥ gaṇāḥ hi ete vīryavantaḥ mahā balāḥ asurāḥ ye tadā teṣām āsan dāyāda bāndhavāḥ suparṇa yakṣa gandharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ aṣṭau tāḥ pitṛbhiḥ sārddham āsan yāḥ devayonayaḥ svāyaṃbhuva intare atītāḥ prajāḥ tāsām mahasraśas prabhāva rūpa saṃpannāḥ āyuṣā ca balena ca atītaḥ vartamānena dṛṣṭaḥ vaivasvate na saḥ prajābhiḥ devātābhiḥ ca ṛṣibhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha teṣām sarpa ṛṣayaḥ pūrvam āsan ye tān nibodhata bhṛgvam girā marīciḥ ca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ āgnīdhraḥ ca agnibāhuḥ ca modhāḥ medhātithiḥ vasuḥ vāyu vegāḥ mahāsattvāḥ rājānaḥ prathameṃ'tare sa piśāca manuṣyam ca sa suparṇa apsaraḥ gaṇam na śakyam ānu pūrvyeṇa vaktum varṣa śataiḥ api bahu tvāt nāmadheyānām saṃkhyā teṣām kutas kule yāḥ vai prajāḥ yuga ākhyāḥ tu āsan svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare kālena mahatā atītāḥ ayana abda yuga kramaiḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kaḥ eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ sarva bhūta apahārakaḥ kasya yoniḥ kimādiḥ ca kim sa tattvaḥ kimātmakaḥ kim asya cakṣuḥ kā mūrtiḥ ke vā avayavāḥ smṛtāḥ kim nāmadheyam kaḥ asya ātmā brūhi tattvataḥ sūtaḥ uvāca śrūyatā kāla sadbhāvaḥ śrutvā ca eva avadhāryatām sūrya yoniḥ nimeṣa ādiḥ saṃkhyācakṣuḥ saḥ ucyate mūrtiḥ asya tu ahaḥ rātraḥ nimeṣa avayavaḥ ca saḥ saṃvatsaraḥ satattvaḥ ca nāma ca asya kalā ātmakaḥ sāmprata an āgata atīta kāla ātmā sa prajāpatiḥ pañcadhā pravibhaktām tu kāla avasthām nibodhata iḍravatsaraḥ tṛtīyaḥ ca caturthaḥ ca anuvatsaraḥ pañcamaḥ vatsaraḥ teṣām kālaḥ sa yuga sajñitaḥ teṣām tattvam pravakṣyāmi kīrtyamānam nibodhata āditeyaḥ tu asau sūryaḥ kālāgniḥ parivatsaraḥ śukla kṛṣṇa gatiḥ ca api apām sāra mayaḥ khagaḥ saḥ iḍā vatsaraḥ somaḥ purāṇe niścayam gataḥ yaḥ ca ayam pavate lokān tanubhiḥ sapta saptabhiḥ ahaṅkārāt udak rudraḥ saṃbhūtaḥ brahmaṇā astu yaḥ sa rudraḥ vatsaraḥ teṣām vijñeyaḥ nīlalohitaḥ aṅga pratyaṅga saṃyogāt kāla ātmā pratitāmahaḥ ṛk sāma yajuṣām yoniḥ pañcānām patiḥ īśvaraḥ saḥ agniḥ yamaḥ ca kālaḥ ca saṃbhūtiḥ sa prajāpatiḥ proktaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ ca iti sūrya coniḥ manīṣibhiḥ yasmāt kāla vibhāgānām māsa ṛtu ayanayoḥ api graha nakṣatra śīta uṣṇa varṣa āyuḥ karmaṇām tathā yoniḥ sa pravibhāgānām divasānām ca bhāskaraḥ vaikārikaḥ prasanna ātmā brahma putraḥ prajāpatiḥ ādityaḥ savitā bhānuḥ jīvanaḥ brahma satkṛtaḥ prabhavaḥ ca avyayaḥ ca eva bhūtānām tena bhāskaraḥ tārā abhimānī vijñeyaḥ dvitīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ ājīvaḥ sarva bhūtānām yogakṣema kṛt īśvaraḥ āvekṣamāṇaḥ satatam bibharti jagat aṃśubhiḥ tithīnām parvasaṃdhīnām pūrṇimā darśayoḥ api yoniḥ niśākaraḥ yaḥ ca amṛta ātmā prajāpatiḥ tasmāt sa pitṛmān somaḥ smṛtaḥ iṅ vatsara ātmakaḥ prāṇa apāna samāna ādyaiḥ vyāna udāna ātmakaiḥ api karmabhiḥ prāṇinām loke sarva ceṣṭā pravartakaḥ pañcānām ca indriya manoḥ buddhi smṛti bala ātmanām samāna kāla karaṇa kriyāḥ saṃpādayan api sarva ātmā sarva loka īśaḥ āvaha pravaha ādibhiḥ vidhātā sarva bhūtānām kṣemī nityam prabhañjanaḥ yoniḥ agneḥ apām bhūmeḥ raveḥ candramasaḥ cayaḥ vāyuḥ prajāpatiḥ bhūtaḥ loka ātmā prapitāmahaḥ ete prajānām patayaḥ catvāraḥ upapakṣa jāḥ pitaraḥ sarva lokānām loka ātmānaḥ prakīrttitāḥ ṛṣiḥ viprāḥ mahādevaḥ bhūtātmā prapitāmahaḥ īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām praṇavaḥ yaḥ ātma āveśena bhūtānām aṅga pratyaṅga saṃbhavaḥ sūryaḥ ca candramāḥ ca agniḥ vāyuḥ rudraḥ tathā eva ca yuga abhimānī kāla ātmā nityam saṃkṣaya kṛt vibhuḥ āśrayāt mayi saṃyogāt tanubhiḥ nāmamiḥ tathā yatas patiḥ sa bhagavān prajā īśānām prajāpatiḥ bhāvanaḥ sarva bhūtānām sarva ātmā nīlalohitaḥ auṣadhīḥ pratisaṃdhatte rudraḥ kṣīṇāḥ punar punar gāyatrī ca eva triṣṭubh ca jagatī ca eva yāḥ smṛtāḥ tryaṃbakāḥ nāmataḥ premṇā yonayaḥ tāḥ vanaspateḥ tābhiḥ eka tva bhūtābhiḥ trividhābhiḥ sva vīryataḥ tri sādhanaḥ puroḍāśaḥ tri kapālaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ tryaṃbakaḥ sa puroḍāśaḥ tena eṣa tryaṃbakaḥ smṛtaḥ iti etat pañca varṣam hi yugam proktam manīṣibhiḥ yaḥ ca eṣa pañcadhā ātmā vai proktaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ dvijaiḥ sa ekaḥ ṣaṭkaḥ vijajñe atha madhu ādi ṛtu saṃjñakaḥ ṛtuputra ārttavāḥ pañca iti sargaḥ samāsatas iti eṣa bahu mānaḥ vai prāṇinā jīvitāni ca nadī vegaḥ iva āsaktaḥ kālaḥ dhāvati saṃharan eteṣām yat apatyam vai tat aśakyam pramāṇataḥ imam vaṃśam prajā īśānām mahataḥ puṇya karmaṇām kīrttayan puṇya kīrttīnām mahatīm siddhim āpnuyāt iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde kālasadbhāvavarṇanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāya atha antareṣu sarveṣu atīta anāgateṣu iha tulya abhimāninaḥ sarve jāyante nāma rūpataḥ devāḥ ca aṣṭavidhāḥ ye ca tasmin mamvantare adhipāḥ mahā ṛṣi sargaḥ saṃkrāntaḥ vaṃśam svāyaṃbhuvasya tu vistareṇa ānupūrvyā ca kīrtya mānam nibodhata manoḥ svāyaṃbhūvasya āsan daśa pautrāḥ tu tad samāḥ yaiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sa pattanā sa samudrā karavatī prativarṣam niveśitā svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare pūrvam ādye tretā yuge tathā priyavratāt prajā upetān vīrān kāmyān vyajāyata kanyā sā tu mahābhāga kardamasya prajā pateḥ kanye dve daśa putrāḥ ca samrāj kukṣiḥ ca te śubhe tayoḥ vai bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ prajāpati samāḥ daśa āgnīdhraḥ ca agnibā huḥ ca medhāḥ medhātithiḥ vasuḥ dvīpeṣu teṣu dharmeṇa dvīpa antāḥ ca nibodhata jaṃbūdvīpa īśvaram cakre āgnīdhram su mahā balam plakṣadvīpa īśvaraḥ ca api tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ śālmale tu vapuṣmantam rājānam saḥ abhiṣiktavān jyotiṣmantam kuśadvīpe rājānam kṛtavān prabhuḥ dyutimantam ca rājānam kraiñcadvīpe abhyaṣecayat śākadvīpa īśvaram ca api havyam cakre priyavrataḥ puṣkara adhipatim ca eva savanam kṛtavān prabhuḥ mahāvītam smṛtam varṣam tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ nāmnā ca dhātakeḥ ca api dhātakīkhaṇḍaḥ ucyate havyaḥ vyajanayat putrān śākadvīpa īśvarān prabhuḥ jaladam ca kumāram ca su kumāram maṇīvakam kumārasya tu kaumāram dvitīyam parikīrtitam sukumāram tṛtīyam tu sukumārasya modakasya api modākam ṣaṣṭham varṣam prakīrttitam teṣām tu nāmabhiḥ tāni sapta varṣāṇi tatra vai kuśalaḥ manonugaḥ cha uṣṇaḥ pāvanaḥ ca andhakārakaḥ teṣām sva nāmabhiḥ deśāḥ kraiñcadvīpa āśrayāḥ śubhāḥ kuśalasya tu deśaḥ abhūta kauśalaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ uṣṇasya uṣṇaḥ smṛtaḥ deśaḥ pāvanasya api pāvanaḥ andhakārasya deśaḥ tu āndhakāraḥ prakīrttitaḥ ete janapadāḥ sapta kraiñcadvīpe tu bhāsvarāḥ udbhijjaḥ veṇumān ca eva vairathaḥ lavaṇaḥ dhṛtiḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākaraḥ ca a pi saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ udbhijjam prathamam varṣam dvitīyam veṇumaṇḍalam tṛtīyam vai rathākāram caturtham lavaṇam smṛtam pañcamam dhṛtimat varṣam ṣaṣṭham varṣam prabhākaram teṣām deśāḥ kaśadvīpe tad sanāmānaḥ eva ca āśrama ācāra yuktābhiḥ prajābhiḥ samalaṅkṛtāḥ śālmalasya īśvarāḥ sapta sutāḥ te ca vapuṣmataḥ śvetaḥ ca haritaḥ ca eva jīmūtaḥ rohitaḥ tathā śvetaḥ tu deśaḥ śvetasya haritasya suhāritaḥ jīmūtasya api jīmūtaḥ rohitasya api rohitaḥ plakṣa dvīpam pravakṣyāmi jaṃbūdvīpāt anantaram sapta medhātithe putrāḥ plakṣadvīpa īśvarāḥ nṛpāḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayaḥ nāma dvitīyaḥ śiśiraḥ smṛtaḥ śivaḥ tu pecamaḥ teṣām kṣemakaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ ucyate dhruvaḥ tu saptamaḥ jñeyaḥ putrāḥ medhātitheḥ smṛtāḥ saptānām nāmabhiḥ teṣām tāni varṣāṇi sapta vai ānandam ca śivam ca eva kṣemakam ca dhruvam tathā tāni teṣām samānāni sapta varṣāṇi bhāgaśas niveśitāni taiḥ tāni pūrvam varṇa āśrama ācāra yuktāḥ plakṣadvīpe prajāḥ kṛtāḥ plakṣadvīpa ādiṣu tu eṣu śākadvīpa antikeṣu vai jñeyaḥ pañcasu dharmaḥ vai varṇa āśrama vibhājakaḥ sukham āyuḥ ca rūpam ca balam dharmaḥ ca nityaśas pañcasu eteṣu dvīpeṣu sarvasādhāḥ raṇam smṛtam prakṣa dvīpaḥ pariṣkrāntaḥ jaṃbūdvīpam nibodhata āgnīdhram jyeṣṭha dāyādam kāmyā putram mahā balam priyavrataḥ abhya siñcat tam jaṃbūdvīpa īśvaram nṛpam jyeṣṭhaḥ nābhiḥ iti khyātaḥ tasya kiṃpuruṣaḥ anujaḥ harivarṣaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu caturthaḥ abhūt ilāvṛtaḥ ramyaḥ tu pañcamaḥ putraḥ hiraṇvān ṣaṣṭhaḥ ucyate kuruḥ tu saptamaḥ teṣām bhadrāśvaḥ ca aṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ navamaḥ ketumālaḥ ca teṣām deśān nibodhata nābheḥ tu dakṣiṇam varṣam hima ākhyam tu pitā dadau hemakūṭam tu yat varṣam dadau kipuruṣāya tat naiṣadham yat smṛtam varṣam harivarṣāya tam dadau nīlam tu yat smṛtam varṣam dadau śvetam yat uttaram tasmāt pitrā dattam hiraṇvate sālyavantam tathā varṣam bhadrāśvāya nyavedayat iti etāni mayā uktāni nava varṣāṇi bhāgaśas ā agnī dhrasteṣu varṣeṣu putrān tān abhyaṣecayat iti etauḥ saptabhiḥ kṛtsnā sapta dvīpāḥ nive śitāḥ evam varṣeṣu sarveṣu sanniveśāḥ punar punar evam svabhāvaḥ kalpānām dvīpānām ca niveśane yāni kiṃpuruṣa ādyāni varṇāṇi aṣṭau śrutāni tu teṣām svabhāvataḥ siddhiḥ sukha prāyam ayatnataḥ dharma adharmaum na teṣu āstāḥ na uttama adhama madhyamāḥ na teṣu asti yuga avasthā kṣetreṣu aṣṭāsu sarvaśas ṛṣabham pārthiva śreṣṭham sarva kṣatrasya pūrvajam ṛṣabhāt bharataḥ jajñe vīraḥ putra śata agrajaḥ saḥ abhiṣicya ṛṣabhaḥ putram mahā pravrajyayā sthitaḥ himāhvam dakṣiṇam varṣam bharatāya nyavedayat tasmāt tu bhāratam varṣam tasya nāmnā viduḥ budhāḥ putra saṃkrāmita śrīḥ tu vanam rājā viveśa saḥ parameṣṭhī sutaḥ ca api nidhane tasya ca api abhūt pratīhāraḥ kulam tasya nāmnā jajñe tad anvayaḥ unnetā pratihartuḥ tu bhūmā tasya sutaḥ smṛtaḥ pṛthoḥ ca api sutaḥ naktaḥ naktasya api gayaḥ sutaḥ virāj sutaḥ mahā vīryaḥ dhīmān tasya sutaḥ abhavat dhīmataḥ ca mahān putraḥ mahataḥ ca api bhauvanaḥ tasya putra śatam tu āsīt rājānaḥ sarve eva tu viśvajyotiḥ pradhānāḥ te yaiḥ imāḥ varddhitāḥ prajāḥ taiḥ idam bhāratam varṣam sapta dvīpam iha aṅkitam teṣām vaṃśa prasūtaiḥ tu bhuktā iyam bhāratī purā kṛta tretā ādi yuktāḥ tu yuga ākhyāḥ hi ekasaptatiḥ ye atītāḥ taiḥ yugaiḥ sārdham rājānaḥ te tad anvayāḥ svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare pūrvam śataśas atha sahasraśas evam svāyam bhuvaḥ sargaḥ yena idam pūritam jagat ṛṣibhiḥ daivataiḥ ca api pirtṛ gandhava rākṣasaiḥ yakṣa bhūta piśācaiḥ ca manuṣya mṛga pakṣibhiḥ teṣām sṛṣṭiḥ iyam proktā yugaiḥ saha vivarttate iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde priyavratavaṃśānukīrttanam nāma catudaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca evam prajā sanniveśam śrutvā vai śāṃśapāyaniḥ kati dvīpā samudrāḥ vā pavatā vā kati smṛtāḥ kiyanti ca eva varṣāṇi teṣu nadyaḥ ca kāḥ smṛtāḥ mahā bhūtapramāṇam ca lokālokam tathā eva ca paryāyam parimāṇam ca gatim candra arkayoḥ tathā sūtaḥ uvāca saṃkhyām ca eva samudrāṇām dvīpānām ca eva vistaram teṣām manuṣyāḥ starkkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣate acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvāḥ na tān tarkeṇa sādhayet nava varṣam pravakṣyāmi jaṃbūdvīpam yathātatham śatam ekam sahasrāṇām yojana agrāt samantataḥ nānā janapada ākīrṇaḥ puraiḥ ca vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃkīṇaḥ parvataiḥ upaśobhitaḥ jaṃbūdvīpaḥ pṛthuḥ śrīmān sarvatas pṛthu maṇḍalaḥ navabhiḥ ca āvṛtaḥ sarvaḥ bhuvanaiḥ bhūta bhāvanaiḥ jaṃbūdvīpasya vistārāt samena tu samantataḥ prāc āyatāḥ sūparvāṇaḥ ṣaṭ ime varṣaparvatāḥ avagāḍhāḥ hi ubhayatas masudrau pūrva paścimau hima prāyaḥ ca himavān hemakūṭaḥ ca hemavān catur varṇaḥ ca sauvarṇaḥ meruḥ cārutamaḥ smṛtaḥ dvātriṃśat ca sahasrāṇi vistīrṇaḥ sa ca mūrddhani vṛtta ākṛti pramāṇaḥ ca catur asraḥ samucchritaḥ nānā varṇāḥ tu pārśveṣu prajāpati guṇa anvitaḥ pūrvataraḥ śveta varṇaḥ ca brāhmaṇaḥ tasya tena tat tena asya kṣattra bhāvaḥ tu meroḥ nānā artha kāraṇāt pītaḥ ca dakṣiṇena asau tena vaiśya tvam iṣyate bhṛṅga patra nibhaḥ ca api paścimena samācitaḥ tena asya śūdra bhāvaḥ syāt iti varṇāḥ prakīrttitāḥ vṛttaḥ svabhāvataḥ proktaḥ varṇataḥ parimāṇataḥ nīlaḥ ca vaidurya mayaḥ śvetaḥ ghuklaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ mayuḥ abarha varṇaḥ tu śātakaiṃbhaḥ ca śṛṅgavān ete parvata rājānaḥ siddha cāraṇa sevitāḥ madhye tu ilāvṛtam nāma mahāmeroḥ samantamaḥ varṣāṇi yāni ṣaḍ ca eva teṣām ye varṣaparvatāḥ dve dve sahasre vistīrṇāḥ yojanānām samucchrayāt jaṃbūdvīpasya vistārāt teṣām āyāmaḥ ucyate yojanānām sahasrāṇi śatam dvau āyatau girī nīlaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ ca eva tābhyām hīnāḥ tu ye pare śvetaḥ ca hemakūṭaḥ ca himavān śṛṅgavān tathā navatī dve aśītī dve sahasrāṇi āyatāḥ tu teḥ teṣām madhye janapadāḥ tāni varṇāṇi sapta vai vasaṃti teṣu sattvāni nānā jātīni sarvaśas idam haimavatam varṣam bhāratam nāma viśrutam hemakūṭam param hi asmāt kiṃṣurupam smṛtam naiṣadham hemakūṭāt tu harivarṣam tat ucyate harivarṣāt param ca api tat ilāvṛtam ilāvṛtāt piram nīlam samyakam nāma viśrutam ramyakāt parataraḥ śvetam viśrutam tat hiraṇmayam hiraṇmayāt param ca eva śṛṅgavattaḥ kuru smṛtam dīrghāṇi tatra catvāri madhyamam tat ilāvṛtam arvāk ca niṣadhasya atha vedyarddham dakṣiṇam smṛtam vedi arddhe dakṣiṇe trīṇi trīṇi varṣāṇi ca uttare udagāya itas mahā śailaḥ mālyavān nāma nāmataḥ yojanānām sahasram tu ānīla niṣadha āyataḥ āyāmataḥ catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi prakīrtitaḥ tasya pratīcyām vijñeyaḥ parvataḥ gandhamādanaḥ āyāmataḥ atha vistārāt mālyavā n iti viśrutaḥ sumeruḥ śuśubhe śubhraḥ rāja vat samadhiṣṭhitaḥ taruṇa āditya varṇa ābhaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt vistṛtaḥ ṣoḍaśa eva tu śarāva saṃsthita tvāt tu dvātriṃśat mūrdhni vistṛtaḥ vistārāt riguṇaḥ tasya pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ maṇḍalena pramāṇena tri asre mānam tat iṣyate catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi yojanānām samantataḥ aṣṭābhiḥ adhikāni syuḥ tri asre mānam prakīrttitam catur asreṇa mānena pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ catuḥ ṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi yojanānām vidhīyate bhuvanaiḥ āvṛtaḥ sarvaḥ jātarūpa mayaiḥ śubhaiḥ tatra deva gaṇāḥ sarve gandharva uraga rākṣasāḥ śailarāje pradṛśyante śubhāḥ ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ catvāraḥ yasya deśāḥ vai catur pārśveṣu adhiṣṭhitāḥ bhadrāśvāḥ bharatāśvā eva ketumālāḥ ca paścimāḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ ca eva kṛta puṇya pratiśrayāḥ gandhamādana parśve tu parā eṣā apara gaṇḍikā sarva ṛttu ramaṇīyā ca nityam pramuditā śivā dvātriṃśat tu sahasrāṇi yojanaiḥ pūrva paścimāt āyāmataḥ catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi pramāṇataḥ tatra te śubha karmāṇaḥ ketumālāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ tatra kālāḥ narāḥ sarve mahāsattvāḥ mahā balāḥ striyaḥ ca utpala patra ābhāḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ priya darśanāḥ tatra divyaḥ mahā vṛkṣaḥ panasaḥ paṣ rasa āśrayaḥ īśvaraḥ brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ kāma cārī manojavaḥ pārśve mālyavataḥ ca api pūrve apūrvā tu gaṇḍikā āyāmāt atha vistārāt yathā eṣā apara gaṇḍikā bhadrāśvāḥ tatra vijñeyāḥ nityam mudita mānasāḥ bhadraśāla vanam ca atra kāla āmraḥ tu mahā drumaḥ tatra te puruṣāḥ svetāḥ mahā utsāhāḥ bala anvitāḥ striyaḥ kumuda varṇa ābhāḥ sundaryaḥ priya darśanāḥ candra prabhāḥ candra varṇāḥ pūrṇa candra nibha ānanāḥ candra śītala gātryaḥ tāḥ striyaḥ utpala gandhikāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi teṣām āyuḥ anāmayam kāla āmrasya rasam pītvā sarve ca sthira yauvanāḥ varṣam ramaṇakam nāma jāyante tatra mānavāḥ śukla abhijana saṃpannāḥ sarve ca priya darśanāḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti te mahābhāgāḥ sadā tdṛṣṭāḥ nara uttamāḥ dakṣiṇe vai śṛṅgavataḥ śvetasya api uttareṇa ca varṣam hairaṇvatam nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadī mahā balāḥ su tejaskāḥ jāyante tatra mānavāḥ yakṣāḥ vīrāḥ mahāsattvāḥ dhaninaḥ priya darśanāḥ ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām te mahā ojasaḥ āyuḥ pramāṇam jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca ca yasmin varṣe mahā vṛkṣaḥ lakucaḥ ṣaṣ rasa āśrayaḥ tasya pītvā phala rasam te jīvanti nirāmayāḥ trīṇi śṛṅgavataḥ śṛṅgāṇi ucchritāni mahānti ca ekam maṇi mayam teṣām ekam ca eva hiraṇmayam uttare vai śṛṅgāvataḥ samudrasya ca dakṣiṇe tatra vṛkṣāḥ madhu phalāḥ nitya puṣpa phala upagāḥ vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣu ābharaṇāni ca sarva kāma pradāḥ tatra kecid vakṣāḥ manoramāḥ apare kṣīriṇaḥ nāma vṛkṣāḥ tatra manoramāḥ ye kṣaranti sadā kṣīram ṣaṣ rasam hi amṛta upamam sarvā maṇi mayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣma kāñcana vālukā sarva ṛtu sukha saṃpannā niṣpaṅkā nīrajā śubhā deva loka cyutāḥ tatra jāyante mānavāḥ śubhāḥ śukla abhijana saṃpannāḥ sarve ca sthira yauvanāḥ mithunāni prasūyante striyaḥ ca apsarasaḥ samāḥ teṣām te kṣīriṇām kṣīram pibanti hi amṛta u pamam samam śīlam ca rūpam ca priya tā ca eva tad samā anāmayāḥ hi aśokāḥ ca nityam sukha niṣeviṇaḥ trayodaśa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti te mahā vīryāḥ na ca anya strī niṣeviṇaḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrva bhāge dvītīye anuṣaṅga pāde pṛthivyāyāmavistaraḥ nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca evam eva nisargaḥ vai varṣāṇām bhārate śubhe dṛṣṭaḥ parama tattva jñaiḥ bhūyas kim varṇayāmi vaḥ ṛṣiḥ uvāca yat idam bhāratam varṣam yasmin svāyaṃbhuva ādayaḥ etat śruta vacaḥ teṣām abravīt romaharṣaṇaḥ atra vaḥ varṇayiṣyāmi varṣe asmin bhārate prajāḥ varṣam tat bhāratam nāma yatra iyam bhāratī prajā nirukta vacanāt ca evam varṣam tat bhāratam smṛtam itas svargaḥ ca mokṣaḥ ca madhyaḥ ca antaḥ ca gamyate samudra ātaritāḥ jñeyāḥ te tu agamyāḥ parasparam indradvīpaḥ kaśerūmān tāmravarṇaḥ gabhastimān nāgadvīpaḥ tathā saumyaḥ gāndharvaḥ tu atha vāruṇaḥ ayam tu navamaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃvṛtaḥ yojanānām sahasre tu dvīpaḥ ayam dakṣiṇa uttarāt āyataḥ hi ā kumāryyāḥ vai ca ā gaṅgā prabhavāt ca vai dvīpaḥ hi upaniviṣṭaḥ ayam mlecchaiḥ anteṣu sarvaśas pūrve kirātāḥ hi asya ante paścime yavanāḥ smṛtāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ madhye śūdrāḥ ca bhāgaśas dharma artha kāma saṃyuktaḥ varṇānām tu sva karmasu saṃkalpaḥ pañcamānām ca hi āśramāṇām yathāvidhi iha svarga apavarga artham pravṛttiḥ yeṣu mānuṣī ayam lokaḥ tu vai samrāj antarikṣam virāj smṛtam svarāj asau smṛtaḥ laukaḥ punar vakṣyāmi vistarāt sapta eva asmin su parvāṇaḥ viśrutāḥ kula parvatāḥ mahendraḥ malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimān ṛkṣa parvataḥ teṣām sahasraḥ ca anye parva tāḥ tu samīpa gāḥ avijñātāḥ sāravantaḥ vipulāḥ citra sānavaḥ saṃdaraḥ parvata śreṣṭhaḥ vaihāraḥ durduraḥ tathā vātandhamaḥ nāgagiriḥ tathā pāṇḍura parvataḥ śrīparvataḥ citrakūṭaḥ kūṭaśailaḥ giriḥ tathā anye tebhyaḥ a parijñātāḥ hrasvāḥ vinaḥ taiḥ vimiśrāḥ janapadāḥ āryāḥ mlecchāḥ ca bhāgaśas pīyante yaiḥ imāḥ nadyaḥ gaṅgā siṃdhu sarasvatī śatadruḥ candra bhāgā ca yamunā sarayūḥ tathā irāvatī vitastā ca vipāśā devikā kuhūḥ gomatī dhūtapāpā ca budbudā ca dṛṣadvatī kauśakī tridivā ca eva niṣṭhīvī geḍakī tathā cakṣurlohitaḥ iti etāḥ himavat pāda nissṛtāḥ varṇāśā nandanā ca eva sadānīrā mahānadī pāśā carmaṇvatī inūpā vidiśā vetravatī api kṣiprāḥ ca tathā pāriyātra āśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ śoṇaḥ mahānadaḥ ca eva narmmadā surasā kriyā mandākinī daśārṇā ca citrakūṭā tathā eva ca tamasā pippalā śyenā karamodā piśācikā citropalā viśālā ca bañjulā vāstuvāhinī sanerujā śuktimatī maṅkutī tridivā kratuḥ ṛkṣa vat saṃprasūtāḥ tāḥ nadyaḥ maṇi jalāḥ śivāḥ tāpī payoṣṇī nirvindhyā sṛpā ca niṣadhā nadī veṇī vaitaraṇī ca eva kṣiprā vālā kumudvatī toyā ca eva mahāgaurī durgā vā annaśilā tathā vindhya pāda prasūtāḥ tāḥ nadyaḥ puṇya jalāḥ śubhāḥ godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇaveṇā atha bañjulā tuṅgabhadrā suprayogā bāhyā kāveḥ yathā api ca dakṣiṇa pravahāḥ nadyaḥ sahya pādāt viniḥsmṛtāḥ kṛtamālā tāmraparṇī puṣpajātī utpalāvatī nadyaḥ abhijātāḥ malayāt sarvāḥ śīta jalāḥ śubhāḥ trisāmā ṛṣikulyā ca bañjulā tridivā abalā lāṅgūlinī vaṃśa dharāḥ mahendra tanayāḥ smṛtāḥ ṛṣikulyā kumārī ca mandagā manda gāminī kṛpā palāśinī ca eva śuktimat prabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ tāḥ tu nadyaḥ sarasvatyaḥ sarvāḥ gaṅgāḥ samudra gāḥ viśvasya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ jagat pāpa harāḥ smṛtāḥ tāsām nadī upanadyaḥ anyāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tāsu ime kuru pāñcālāḥ śālvāḥ mādreya jāṅgalāḥ śūrasenāḥ bhadrakārāḥ bodhāḥ sahapaṭaccarāḥ matsyāḥ kuśalyāḥ sauśalyāḥ kuntalāḥ kāśi kośalāḥ godhāḥ bhadrāḥ kariṅgāḥ ca māgadhāḥ ca utkalaiḥ saha madhyadeśyāḥ janapadāḥ prāyaśasttra kīrttitāḥ pṛthivyām api kṛtsnāyām sa pradeśaḥ manoramaḥ svargīyāḥ vāhlīkāḥ vāṭadhānāḥ ca ābhīrā kālatoyakāḥ aparāntāḥ ca muhmāḥ ca pāñcalāḥ carma maṇḍalāḥ gāndhārāḥ yavanāḥ ca eva siṃdhusauvīra maṇḍalāḥ cīnāḥ ca eva tuṣārāḥ ca pallavāḥ giri gahvarāḥ śākāḥ bhadrāḥ kulindāḥ ca pāradāḥ vindhyacūlikāḥ abhīṣāhāḥ ulūtāḥ ca kekayāḥ daśāmālikāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ ca eva vaiśya śūdra kulāni tu kāṃvojāḥ daradāḥ ca eva barbarāḥ aṅgalauhikāḥ atrayaḥ sa bharadvājāḥ prasthalāḥ ca daśerakāḥ lamakāḥ tālaśālāḥ ca bhūṣikāḥ ījikaiḥ saha ete deśāḥ udīcyāḥ vai prācyān deśān nibodhata aṅga vaṅgāḥ ścolabhadrāḥ kirātānām ca jātayaḥ tomarāḥ haṃsabhaṅgāḥ ca kāśmīrāḥ taṅgaṇāḥ tathā jhillikāḥ ca āhukāḥ ca eva hūṇadarvāḥ tathā eva ca tatas plavaṅgavaḥ jñeyāḥ maladāḥ mala vartikāḥ samantarāḥ prāvṛṣeyāḥ bhārgavāḥ gopa pārthivāḥ prāgjyotiṣāḥ ca puṇḍrāḥ ca videhāḥ tāmraliptakāḥ mallāḥ magadha gonardāḥ prācyām janapadāḥ smṛtāḥ atha apare janapadāḥ dakṣiṇāpatha vāsinaḥ paṇḍyāḥ ca keralāḥ ca eva colāḥ kulyāḥ tathā eva ca setukāḥ mūṣikāḥ ca eva kṣapaṇāḥ vanavāsikāḥ māharāṣṭrāḥ mahiṣikāḥ kaliṅgaḥ ca eva sarvaśas ābhīrāḥ ca saha eṣīkāḥ āṭavyā sāravāḥ tathā pulindāḥ vindhyamaulīyāḥ vaidarbhāḥ daṇḍakaiḥ saha paurikāḥ maulikāḥ ca eva śmakāḥ koṅkaṇāḥ kantalāḥ ca andhrāḥ kulinda aṅgāra māriṣāḥ dākṣiṇāḥ ca eva ye deśāḥ aparān tān nibodhata sūryyārakāḥ kalivanāḥ durgālāḥ kuntarauḥ sahaḥ pauleyāḥ ca kirātāḥ ca rūpakāḥ tāpakaiḥ saha nāsikāḥ ca eva ye ca anye ye ca eva antara narmadāḥ sahakacchāḥ samāheyāḥ saha sārasvataiḥ api kacchipāḥ ca surāṣṭrāḥ ca ānartāḥ ca arbudaiḥ saha iti ete apara antāḥ ca śṛṇudhvam vindhya vāsinaḥ maladāḥ ca karūthāḥ ca mekalāḥ caitkalaiḥ saha uttamānām daśārṇāḥ ca bhojāḥ kiṣkindhakaiḥ saha tośalāḥ kośalāḥ ca eva traipurāḥ vaidiśāḥ tathā tuhuṇḍāḥ barbarāḥ ca eva ṣaṣ purāḥ naiṣadhaiḥ saha anūpāḥ tuṇḍikerāḥ ca vītihotrāḥ hi avantayaḥ ete janapadāḥ sarve vindhya pṛṣṭha nivāsinaḥ atas deśān pravakṣyāmi parvata āśrayiṇaḥ ca ye nihīrāḥ haṃsamārgāḥ ca kupathāḥ taṅgaṇāḥ śakāḥ apaprāva raṇāḥ ca eva ūrṇāḥ darvāḥ sahūhukāḥ trigarttāḥ maṇḍalāḥ ca eva kirātāḥ tāmaraiḥ saha catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni ṛṣayaḥ abruvan kṛtam tretā yugam ca eva dvāparam tiṣyam eva ca teṣām nisargam vakṣyāmi upariṣṭāt aśeṣatas iti śrī bradṛ mahāpurāṇe vāyu prokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde bhāratavarmatam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ yat ca kiṃpuruṣam varṣam harivarṣam tathā eva ca ācakṣva naḥ yathātattvam kīrttitam bhāratam tvayā sūtaḥ uvāca śuśrūṣā yatra vaḥ viprāḥ tat śṛṇudhvam atandritāḥ plakṣakhaṇḍaḥ kiṃpuruṣe su mahān nandana upamaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi sthitiḥ kiṃpuruṣe smṛtā suvarṇa varṇāḥ puruṣāḥ striyaḥ ca apsarasaḥ upamāḥ anāmayāḥ aśokāḥ ca nityam mudita mānasāḥ varṣe kiṃpuruṣe puṇye vṛkṣaḥ madhu vahaḥ śubhaḥ tatas param kiṃpuruṣaḥ harivarṣaḥ pracakṣate mahārajata saṃkāśāḥ jāyante tatra mānavāḥ deva loka cyutāḥ sarve deva anūkāḥ ca sarva īśaḥ harivarṣe narāḥ sarve pibanti ikṣu rasam śupham ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām tu nirāmayāḥ madhyamam yat mayā proktam nāmnā varṣam ilāvṛtam candra sūryaiḥ sa nakṣatrau na prakāśau ilā vṛte padma prabhāḥ padba varṇāḥ tathā padba nibha īkṣaṇāḥ padma patra sugandhāḥ ca jāyante tatra mānavāḥ jaṃbū phala rasa āhārāḥ a nisyandāḥ su gandhinaḥ trayodaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām te nara uttamāḥ āyuḥ pramāṇam jīvanti ye tu varṣe ilāvṛte yojanānām sahasrāṇi ṣaṭtriṃśat tasya vistaraḥ yaturasram samantāt ca śarāva ākāra saṃsthitam udak dakṣiṇatas ca eva ā nīla niṣadha āyataḥ catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi parivṛddhaḥ mahī talāt sahasram avagāḍhaḥ ca tāvat eva ca vistṛtaḥ pūrveṇa mālyavān śailaḥ tad pramāṇaḥ prakīrttitaḥ dakṣiṇena tu nīlaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ ca uttareṇa tu teṣām madhye mahā meruḥ svaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ sarveṣām eva śailānām avagāḍhaḥ yathā bhavet vistaraḥ tad pramāṇaḥ syāt āyāmaḥ niyutam smṛtaḥ vṛtta bhāvāḥ samudrasya mahī maṇḍala bhāvataḥ āyāmāḥ parihīyante catur asra samāḥ smṛtāḥ ilāvṛtam catuṣkoṇam bhindantī madhya bhāgataḥ prabhinna añjana saṃkāśā jambū rasavatī nadī meroḥ tu dakṣiṇe pārśve niṣadhasya uttareṇa ca sudarśanaḥ nāma mahān jambu vṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ tasya nāmnā samā khyātaḥ jambūdvīpaḥ vanaspateḥ yojanānām sahasram ca śatam ca anyat mahātmanaḥ utsedhaḥ vṛkṣarājasya divam spṛśati sarvatas aratnīnām śatāni aṣṭau ekaṣaṣṭi adhikāni tu phala pramāṇam saṃkhyātam ṛṣibhiḥ tattva darśibhiḥ merum pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā jambu mūlam viśati adhas tam pibanti sadā tdṛṣṭāḥ jaṃbū rasam ilāvṛte jaṃbū phala rase pīte na jarā bādhate tu tān tatra jāṃbūnadam nāma kanakam deva bhūṣamam indragopaka saṃkāśam jāyate bhāsvaram tu tat sarveṣām varṣa vṛkṣāṇām śubhaḥ phala rasaḥ stutaḥ teṣām mūtram purīṣam ca dikṣu sarvāsu sarvaśas īśvara anugrahāt bhūmiḥ mṛtāḥ ca grasate tu tān rakṣaḥ piśāca yakṣāḥ ca sarve haimavataḥ smṛtāḥ hemakūṭe tu gandharvāḥ vijñeyāḥ sa apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ sarve nāgaḥ tu niṣadhe śeṣa vāsuki takṣakāḥ mahā merau trayastriṃśat krīḍante yajñiyāḥ surāḥ nīle tu vaidūrya maye siddhāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ amalāḥ daityānām dānavānām car śvetaḥ parvataḥ ucyate śṛṅgavān parvata śreṣṭhaḥ pitṝṇām pratisaṃcaraḥ navasu eteṣu varṣeṣu yathābhāgam sthiteṣu vai bhūtāni upaniviṣṭāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca teṣām vivṛddhiḥ bahudhā dṛśyate divya mānuṣī na saṃkhyā parisaṃkhyātum śraddheyā tu bubhūṣatām iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde kiṃpuruṣādivarṣavarṇanam nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca madhye himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe kailāsaḥ nāma parvataḥ tasmin nivasati śrīmān kuberaḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ kailāsa pādāt saṃbhūtam puṇyam śīta jalam śubham tasmāt divyāt prabhavati nadī mandākinī śubhā yakṣa senāpatiḥ krūraḥ guhyakaiḥ parivāritaḥ puṇyā mandākinī ca eva nadī svacchodakā ca yā kailāsāt dakṣiṇe prācyām śiva sattva oṣadhim girim manaḥ śilā mayam divyam citrāṅgam parvatam prati lohitaḥ hemaśṛṅgaḥ ca giriḥ sūrya prabhaḥ mahān deva araṇyam viśokam ca tasya tīre mahat vanam kailāsāt dakṣiṇe pārśve krūra sattva oṣadhiḥ giriḥ tasya pāde kalaḥ puṇyam mānasam siddha sevitam tasmāt prabhavete puṇyā sarayūḥ loka viśrutā tasyāḥ tīre vana divyam vaibhrājam nāma viśrutam apareṇa tu kailāsāt puṇya sattva oṣadhiḥ giriḥ aruṇaḥ parvata śreṣṭhaḥ rukma dhātu mayaḥ śubhaḥ śātakaiṃbha mayaiḥ śubhraiḥ śilā jālaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ śātasaṃkhyaiḥ tāpanīyaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ divam iva ullikhan muñjavāstu mahā divyaḥ durgaḥ śailaḥ hima ācitaḥ tasyāḥ pādāt prabhavati śailodam nāma tat saraḥ tasmāt prabhavate puṇyā śilodā nāma nimragā sā cakṣuḥ sītayoḥ madhye praviṣṭā lavaṇa udadhim tasyāḥ tīre vanam divyam viśrutam surabhi iti vai gauram nāma giri śreṣṭham haritāla mayam prati hiraṇyaśṛṅgaḥ su mahān divyaḥ maṇi mayaḥ giriḥ tasyāḥ pāde mahāt divyam śubham kāñcana vālukam ramyam bindusaraḥ nāma yatra rājā bhagīrathaḥ gaṅga nimittam rājarṣiḥ uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ madīyaḥ iti niścitya samāhita manāḥ śive tatra tripayagā devī prathamam tu pratiṣṭhitā soma pādāt prasūtā sā saptadhā pratipadyate yūpāḥ maṇi mayāḥ tatra vitatāḥ ca hiraṇmayāḥ tatra iṣṭvā tu gataḥ siddhim śakraḥ sarvaiḥ suraiḥ saha divi chāyāpathaḥ yaḥ tu anu nakṣatra maṇḍalaḥ dṛśyate bhāsvaraḥ rātrau devī tripathagā tu sā antarikṣam divam ca eva bhāvayantī surāpagā bhava uttamāṅge patitā saṃrūddhā yaugamāyayā cintayāmāsa manasā śaṅkara kṣepamam prati bhittvā viśāmi pātālam srotasā āgṛhya śaṅkaram jñātvā tamyāḥ abhiprāyam krūram devyāḥ cikīrṣitam tirobhāvayitum buddhiḥ āsīt aṅgeṣu tām nadīm tasya avalepam jñātvā tu nadyāḥ kruddhaḥ tu śaṅkaraḥ nyarupāt ca śirasi enām vegena patatīm bhuvi etasmin eva kāle tu dṛṣṭvā rājānam agratas dhamanī saṃtatam kṣīṇam kṣudhayā vyākula indriyam anena toṣitaḥ ca aham nadī artham pūrvam eva tu buddha asya vara dānam ca kopam niyatavān tu saḥ brahmaṇaḥ vacanam śrutvā dhāraya svarṇadīm iti tatas visarjayāmāsa saṃruddhām svena tejasā nadīm bhagīrathasya arthe tapasā ugreṇa toṣitaḥ tatas visṛjyamānāyāḥ srotaḥ tat saptadhā gatam tisraḥ pratīcīm tisraḥ eva tu nadyāḥ srotaḥ tu gaṅgāyāḥ pratyapadyata saptadhā nalinī hlādinī ca eva pāvanī ca eva prācyagāḥ sītā cakṣuḥ ca sindhuḥ ca pratīcīn diśam āsthitāḥ saptamī tu anvagāt tāsām dakṣiṇena bhagīratham tasmāt bhāgīrathī yā sā praviṣṭā lavaṇa udadhim saptā etāḥ bhāvayanti idam himāhvam varṣam eva tu prasūtāḥ sapta nadyaḥ tāḥ śubhāḥ bindu sarā udbhavāḥ nānā deśān plāvayantyaḥ mala iccha prāyāḥ tu sarvaśas upagacchanti tāḥ sarvāḥ yatas varṣati vāsavaḥ śilīndhrān kunta lān cīnān barbarān yavana ādhrakān puṣkarāḥ ca kulindān ca ye kṛtvā tridhā siṃhavantam sītā agāt paścima uda atha cīna marūn ca eva tālān ca masamūlikān bhadrāḥ tuṣārān lāmyākān bāhlavān pāraṭān khaśān etān janapadām ścakṣuḥ prāvayantī gata udadhim daradān ca sa kāśmīrān gāndharān raurasān kuhān śiva śailān indra padān vasatīḥ ca visarjamān saindhavān randhrakara kāñchamaṭha ābhīra rohakān śunā asukhān ca ūrddhamarūn sindhuḥ etān niṣevate kalāpa grāmakān ca eva pāradān tad gaṇān khaśān kirātān ca pulindān ca kurūn sa bharatān api pañcālān kāśi matsyān śca magadha aṅgān tathā eva ca suhma uttarān ca vaṅgān ca tāmraliptān tathā eva ca etān janapadān mānyān gaṅgā bhāvayate śubhān tatas pratihatāḥ vindhyāt praviṣṭāḥ lavaṇa udadhim tatas ca hlādinī puṇya prācīm abhimukhā yayau prāvayanti upabhāgān ca naiṣadhān ca trigarta kān dhīvarān ṛṣikān ca eva tathā nīla mukhān api kekarān auṣṭakarṇān ca kirātān api ca eva hi kālodarān vivarṇāḥ ca kumārān svarṇabhūmikān āmaṇḍalam samudrasya tirobhūtān ca pūrvatas tatas tu pāvanī ca api prācīm eva diśam yayau tathā khara pathān ca eva vetra śaṅku pathān api indradvīpa samudram tu praviṣṭām lavaṇa udadhim tatas tu nalinī prāyāt prācīm āśām javena tu tomarān bhāvayanti iha haṃsa mārgān sa haihayān pūrvan deśān ca sevantī bhittvā sā bahudhā girīn karṇa prāvaraṇān prāpya saṃgatyā śva mukhān api naga maṇḍala madhyena praviṣṭāḥ lavaṇa udadhim tāsām nadī upanadyaḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas upagacchanti tāḥ sarvāḥ yatas varṣati vāsavaḥ hiraṇyaśṛṅge vasati vidvān kauberakaḥ vaśī yajña upetaḥ ca su mahān amita ojāḥ su vikramaḥ kubera anucarāḥ hi ete catvāraḥ tu samāḥ smṛtāḥ evam eva tu vijñeyā ṛddhiḥ parvata vāsinām paraspareṇa dviguṇāḥ dharmataḥ kāmataḥ ṛṛthataḥ hemakūṭasya pṛṣṭhe tu varcovat nāmataḥ saraḥ tasmāt dvayam prabhavati gāndharvī nākulī ca taiḥ tatra jaṃbūnadī puṇyā yasyāḥ jāṃbūnadam smṛtam payaḥ dam tu saraḥ nīle su śubhram puṇḍarīka vat tasmāt nadyau vinirgate śvetāt pravarttate puṇyam sarayūḥ mānasāt dhruvam jyotsnā ca mṛgākāmā ca tasmāt dve saṃbabhūvatuḥ saraḥ kuruṣu vikhyātam padma mīna dvija ākulam anye ca api atra vikhyātāḥ padmā mīna dvija ākulāḥ nāmnā hradāḥ jayāḥ nāma dvādaśa udadhi sannibhāḥ tebhyaḥ śāntā ya mādhvī ca dve nadyau saṃbabhūvatuḥ yāni kiṃpuruṣa ādyāni teṣu devaḥ na varṣati ṛṣabhaḥ dundubhiḥ ca eva dhūmnaḥ ca su mahā giriḥ pūrva āyatā mahā parvā nimagnā lavaṇābhasi candraḥ kākaḥ tathā droṇaḥ su mahāntaḥ śiloccayāḥ udak yātāḥ udīcyāntāḥ avagāḍhāḥ mahā udadhim somakaḥ ca varāhaḥ ca nāradaḥ ca mahīdharaḥ pratīcyām āyatāḥ te vai praviṣṭāḥ lavaṇa udadhima āyatāḥ te mahā śailāḥ samudram dakṣiṇam prati cakra mainākayoḥ madhya vidiśam dakṣiṇām prati nāmnā samudravāsaḥ tu aurvaḥ sa vaḍavāmukhaḥ dvādaśā ete praviṣṭāḥ hi parvatāḥ lavaṇa udadhim yat etat dṛśyate candre śvete kṛṣṇa śaśa ākṛti uttarottaram eteṣām varṣam uddiśyate guṇaiḥ ārogya āyuḥ pramāṇānām dharmataḥ kāmataḥ ṛṛthataḥ samanvitāni bhūtāni puṇyaiḥ etaiḥ tu bhāgaśas vasaṃti nānā jātīni teṣu varṣeṣu tāni vai iti eṣā dhārayantī idam pṛthvī viśvam jagat sthitam iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyu prokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde jambūdvīpavarṇanam nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca plakṣadvīpam pravakṣyāmi yathāvat iha saṃgrahāt śṛṇuta imam yathātattvam bruvataḥ me dvijottamāḥ jaṃbūdvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇāḥ tasya vistaraḥ vistarāt dviguṇaḥ ca asya pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ tena āvṛtaḥ samudraḥ vai dvīpena lavaṇa udakaḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cirāt na mriyate janaḥ kṛte eva ca durbhikṣam jarā vyādhi bhayam kutas tatra api parvatāḥ puṇyāḥ sapta eva maṇi bhūṣaṇāḥ ratna ākarāḥ tathā nadyaḥ tāsām nāmāni ca blakṣadvīpa ādiṣu tu eṣu sapta sapta tu pañcasu ṛju āyatāḥ pratidiśam niviṣṭāḥ varṣaparvatāḥ plakṣadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi sapta dvīpān mahā balān khyāyate yasya nāmnā tu varṣam gomeda saṃjñitam dvitīyaḥ parvataḥ candraḥ aśvibhyām amṛtasya artham oṣadhyaḥ yatra saṃbhṛtāḥ tṛtīyaḥ nāradaḥ nāma durgaśailaḥ mahā uccayaḥ chanda mṛtyuḥ purā tasmin dundubhiḥ sāditaḥ suraiḥ rajju dolā uru kāmam yaḥ śālmaliḥ ca asura antakṛt pañcamaḥ somakaḥ nāma devaiḥ yatra amṛtam purā saṃbhṛtam ca āhṛtam ca eva mātuḥ arthe garutmatā ṣaṣṭaḥ tu sumanāḥ nāma saptama ṛṣabhaḥ ucyate hiraṇyakṣaḥ varāheṇa tasmin śaile niṣūditaḥ vaibhrājaḥ saptamaḥ tatra bhrājiṣṇuḥ sphāṭikaḥ mahān teṣām varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi nāmataḥ tu yathākramam gomedam prathamam varṣam nāmnā aśāntabhayam smṛtam ānandam dundubheḥ varṣam somakasya aśivam smṛtam kṣemakam vṛṣabhasya api vaibhrājasya dhruvam tathā eteṣu deva gandharvāḥ siddhāḥ ca saha cāraṇaiḥ viharanti ramante ca dṛśyamānāḥ ca taiḥ saha teṣām nadyaḥ tu sapta eva prativarṣam samudra gāḥ nāmataḥ tāḥ pravakṣyāmi sapta gaṅgāḥ tapodhanāḥ anutaptā asukhī ca eva vipāśā tridivā kramuḥ amṛtā sukṛtā ca eva saptā etāḥ saritām varāḥ abhigacchanti tāḥ nadyaḥ tābhyaḥ ca anyāḥ sahasraśas tāḥ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭāḥ nadī janapadāḥ tu te śubhāḥ śānta bhayāḥ ca eva pramudam śaiśirāḥ śivāḥ ānandāḥ ca sukhāḥ ca eva kṣemakāḥ ca dhruvaiḥ saha varṇa āśrama ācāra yutā prajāḥ teṣu avadhiṣṭhitāḥ sarve tu arogāḥ su balāḥ prajāḥ ca āmaya va rjitāḥ plakṣadvīpa ādiṣu jñeyaḥ pañcasu eteṣu sarvaśas deśasya anuvidhānena kālasya anuvidhāḥ smṛtāḥ pañca varṣa sahasrāṇi teṣu jīvanti mānavāḥ surūpāḥ ca su veṣāḥ ca hi arogāḥ balinaḥ tathā plakṣadvīpa ādiṣu jñeyaḥ śākadvīpa antikeṣu vai prakṣa dvīpaḥ pṛthuḥ śrīmān sarvatas dhana dhānyavān āvṛtaḥ paśubhiḥ sarvaiḥ grāmya āraṇyaiḥ sahasraśas jaṃbū vṛkṣa ima saṃkhyātaḥ tasya madhye dvijottamāḥ plakṣaḥ nāma mahā vṛkṣaḥ tasya nāmnā saḥ ucyate sa ca api ikṣu rasa udena prakṣa dvīpaḥ samāvṛtaḥ iti evam saṃniveśaḥ vaḥ plakṣadvīpasya kīrtitaḥ ānupūrvyāt samāsena śālmalam tu nibodhata tatas tṛtīyam vakṣyāmi śālmalam dvīpa suttamam plakṣadvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇena samāvṛtaḥ tatra api parvatāḥ sapta vijñeyāḥ ratna yonayaḥ ratna ākarāḥ tathā nadyaḥ teṣām varṣeṣu saptasu prathamaḥ sūrya saṃkāśaḥ kumudaḥ nāma parvataḥ sarva dhātu mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ śilā jāla samākulaiḥ dvitīyaḥ parvataḥ ca atra hi uttamaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ haritāla mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati jāti añjana mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati viśalyakaraṇī ca eva mṛtasañjīvinī tathā nitya puṣpa phala upetaḥ vṛkṣa vīrudh samāvṛtaḥ tatra ratnāni anekāni svayam rakṣati vāsavaḥ iti ete parvatāḥ sapta śālmale maṇi bhūṣaṇāḥ teṣām varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi sarpa eva tu śubhāni vai balāhakasya jīmūtam droṇasya haritam smṛtam varṣāṇi parvatāḥ ca eva nadīḥ teṣu nibodhata jyotiḥ śāntiḥ tathā tuṣṭā candrā śukrā vimocanī nivṛttiḥ saptamī tāsām prativarṣam tu tāḥ smṛtāḥ tāsām samīpa gāḥ ca anyāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas na saṃkhyām parisaṃkhyātum śaknuyāt kaḥ api mānavaḥ iti eṣa saṃniveśaḥ vaḥ śālmalasya prakīrttitaḥ plakṣa vṛkṣeṇa saṃkhyātaḥ tasya madhye mahā drumaḥ śālmalaḥ tu samudreṇa surodena samāvṛtaḥ uttareṣu tu dharma jñāḥ dvīpeṣu śṛṇuta prajāḥ yathāśrutam yathānyāyam bruvataḥ me nibodhata kuśadvīpam pravakṣyāmi caturtham tu samāsatas surā udakaḥ parivṛtaḥ kuśadvīpena sarvatas śālmalasya tu vistārāt dviguṇena samantataḥ kuśadvīpe tu vijñeyaḥ parvataḥ vidrumaḥ ca yaḥ tṛtīyaḥ dyutimān nāma jīmūta sadṛśaḥ giriḥ caturthaḥ puṣpavān nāma pañcamaḥ tu kuśeśayaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ harigiriḥ nāma saptamaḥ mandaraḥ smṛtaḥ mandāḥ iti hi apāḥ nāma mandaraḥ dāraṇāt ayam teṣām antara viṣa kaṃbhaḥ dviguṇaḥ pravibhāgataḥ udbhidam prathamam varṣam dvitīyam veṇumaṇḍalam tṛtīyam vai rathākāram caturtham lavaṇam samṛtam pañcamam dhṛtimat varṣam ṣaṣṭham varṣam prabhākaram saptamam kapilam nāma sarve te varṣa bhāvakāḥ eteṣu deva gandharvāḥ prajāḥ tu jagat īśvarāḥ viharanti ramante ca hṛṣyamāṇāḥ tu sarvaśas tatra api nadyaḥ sapta eva dhūta pāpa aśivā tathā pavitrā saṃtatiḥ ca eva vidyuddaṃbhāḥ mahī tathā anyāḥ tābhyaḥ a parijñātāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas abhigacchanti tāḥ sarvāḥ yatas varṣati vāsavaḥ ghṛtodena kuśadvīpaḥ bāhyatas parivāritaḥ vijñeyaḥ sa tu vistārāt kuśa dvīpa samena tu iti eṣa sanniveśaḥ vaḥ kuśadvīpasya kīrttitaḥ kraiñcadvīpasya vistāram vakṣyāmi aham atas param kuśadvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇaḥ sa tu vai smṛtaḥ tasmin dvīpe naga śreṣṭhaḥ kraiñcaḥ tu prathamaḥ giriḥ kraiñcāt paraḥ vāmanakaḥ vāmanāt andhakārakaḥ andhakārāt paraḥ ca api divāvṛt nāma parvataḥ divāvṛtaḥ paraḥ ca api dvividaḥ giri sattamaḥ dvividāt paratas ca api puṇḍarīkaḥ mahā giriḥ puṇḍarīkāt paraḥ ca api procyate dundubhisvanaḥ bahu puṣpa phala upeta nānā vṛkṣa latā āvṛtāḥ paraspareṇa dviguṇāḥ vistṛtāḥ harṣa varddhanāḥ varṣāṇi tatra vakṣyāmi nāmataḥ tān nibodhata manonugāt paraḥ ca uṣṇaḥ tṛtīyam varṣam ucyate uṣṇāt paraḥ pīvarakaḥ pīvarāt andhakārakaḥ andhakārāt paraḥ ca api munideśaḥ smṛtaḥ budhaiḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃkīrṇaḥ gaura prayaḥ janaḥ smataḥ tatra api nadyaḥ sapta eva prativarṣa smṛtāḥ śubhāḥ gaurī kumudvatī ca eva saṃdhyā rātriḥ manojavā khyātiḥ ca puṇḍarīkā ca gaṅgāḥ saptavidhāḥ smṛtāḥ tāsām sahasraśas ca anyāḥ nadyaḥ yāḥ tu samīpa gāḥ abhigacchanti tāḥ sarvāḥ vipulāḥ su bahu udakāḥ āvṛtaḥ sarvatas śrīmān kraiñcadvīpa samena tu plakṣadvīpa ādayaḥ hi ete samāsena prakīrttitāḥ teṣām nisargaḥ dvīpānām ānupūrvyeṇa sarvaśas nisargaḥ yaḥ prajānām tu saṃhāraḥ yaḥ ca tāsu vai śākadvīpam pravakṣyāmi yathāvat iha niścayāt śṛṇudhvam tu yathātathyam bruvataḥ me yathārthavat kraiñca dvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇāḥ tasya vistaraḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cirāt tu mriyate janaḥ kutas eva ca durbhikṣam jarā vyādhi bhayam kutas tatra api parvatāḥ śabhrāḥ sapta eva maṇi bhūṣaṇāḥ ratna ākarāḥ tathā nadyaḥ teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu prāc āyataḥ sa sauvarṇaḥ hi udayaḥ nāma parvataḥ vṛṣṭi artham jaladāḥ tatra ca yānti ca tasya apareṇa su mahān jaladhāraḥ mahā giriḥ tatas varṣam prabhavati varṣā kāle prajāsu iha revatī divi nakṣatram pitāmaha kṛtaḥ vidhiḥ tasya apareṇa su mahān śyāmaḥ nāma mahā giriḥ tasmāt śyāma tvam āpannāḥ prajāḥ pūrvam imāḥ kila tasya apareṇa su mahān nājataḥ astagiriḥ smṛtaḥ tasya apare ca āṃbikeyaḥ durgaśailaḥ mahā giriḥ udayāt prathamam varṣam mahāt tat jaladam smṛtam raivatasya tu kaumāram śyāmasya ca maṇīvakam astasya api śubham varṣam vijñeyam kusumottaram śākaḥ nāma mahā utsedhaḥ tasya pūjyāḥ mahā anugāḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ cāturvarṇya samanvitāḥ nadyaḥ ca api mahā puṇyāḥ gaṅgāḥ saptavidhāḥ tathā sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī veṇukā ca yā ikṣuḥ ca veṇukā ca eva gabhastiḥ saptamī tathā nadyaḥ ca anyāḥ puṇya jalāḥ śīta toya vahāḥ śubhāḥ sahasraśas samākhyātāḥ yatas varṣati vāsavaḥ na tāsām nāmadheyāni parimāṇam tathā eva ca śakyam vai parisaṃkhyātum puṇyāḥ tāḥ sarit uttamāḥ tāḥ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭāḥ nadīḥ janapadāḥ tu te śāṃśapāyana vistīrṇaḥ dvīpaḥ asau cakra saṃsthitaḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpa phala upetaiḥ samantāt dhana dhānyavān kṣīrodena samudreṇa sarvatas parivāritaḥ śākadvīpasya vistārāt samena tu tasmin janapadāḥ puṇyāḥ parvatāḥ saritaḥ śubhāḥ varṇa āśrama samākīrṇāḥ deśāḥ te sapta vai smṛtāḥ na saṃkaraḥ ca teṣu asti varṇa āśrama kṛtaḥ kvacid dharmasya ca avyabhīcārāt ekānta sukhitāḥ prajāḥ na teṣu lobhaḥ māyā vā hīrṣā asūyā kṛtaḥ kutas viparyayaḥ na teṣu asti kālāt svābhāvikam param kara avāptiḥ na teṣu asti na daṇḍaḥ na ca daṇḍyakāḥ etāvat eva śakyam vai tasmin dvīpe prabhāṣitum etāvat eva śrotavyam śākadvīpa nivāsinām puṣkaram saptamam dvīpam pravakṣyāmi nibodhata puṣkareṇa tu dvīpena vṛtaḥ kṣīra udakaḥ bahis śākadvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇena saṃmatataḥ puṣkare parvataḥ śrīmān ekaḥ eva mahā śilaḥ citraiḥ maṇi mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ śilā jālaiḥ samucchritaḥ sa maṇḍala sahasrāṇi vistīrṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ urddham ca eva catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi mahī talāt yojanānām sahasrāṇi ūrdhvam pañcāśat ucchritaḥ tāvat eva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvatas parimaṇḍalaḥ saḥ eva dvīpa paśca arddhe mānasaḥ pṛthivīdharaḥ ekaḥ eva mahā sāraḥ sanniveśaḥ dvidhā kṛtaḥ svādu udakena udadhinā sarvatas parivāritaḥ puṣkara dvīpa vistārāt vistīrṇaḥ asau samantataḥ mahāvītam tu yat varṣa bāhyatas mānasasya tat dhātakīkhaṇḍam ucyate daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi tatra jīvati mānavāḥ arogāḥ sukha bāhulyāḥ mānasīm siddhim āsthitāḥ masasā āyuḥ ca rūpam ca tasmin varṣa dvaye smṛtam adhama uttamā na teṣu asti tulyāḥ te rūpa śīlataḥ na tatra dasyuḥ damakaḥ na īrṣyā asūyā bhayam tathā varṇa āśramau vā vārtā vā pāśupālyam vaṇikpathaḥ trayī vidyā daṇḍanītiḥ śuśrūṣā śilpam eva ca na tatra varṣam nadyaḥ vā śīta uṣṇam vā api vidyate uttarāṇām kurūṇām ca tulya kālaḥ janaḥ tathā iti eṣa dhātakīkhaṇḍe mahā vīte tathā eva ca ānupūrvyāt vidhiḥ kṛtsnaḥ puṣkarasya prakīrttitaḥ svādu udakena udadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva puṣkarasya samena tu evam dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ tu sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ evam dvīpa samudrāṇām vṛddhiḥ jñeyā parasparāt apām ca eva samudrekāt sāmudraḥ iti saṃjñitaḥ tasmāt varṣam iti proktam prajānām sukha dam yatas ṛṣaḥ iti eṣa ramaṇe vṛṣa śakti prabandhane śuklapakṣe candra vṛddhyā samudraḥ pūryate sadā prakṣīyamāṇe bahule kṣīyate astamite khage āpūryamāṇaḥ hi udadhiḥ svatas eva abhipūryate tathā upakṣīyamāṇe api sva ātmani eva avakṛṣyate ukhā stham agni saṃyogāt udriktam dṛśyate yathā anyūna anatiriktān ca varndvati apaḥ hrasaṃti ca udaya astamaye tu indau pakṣayoḥ śukla kṛṣṇayoḥ kṣaya vṛddha tvam udadheḥ soma vṛddhi kṣayāt punar daśa uttarāṇi pañca eva hi aṅgulāni śatāni ca apām vṛddhiḥ kṣayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sāmudrīṇām tu parvasu dvis āpka tvāt smṛtāḥ dvīpāḥ sarvatas ca udaka āvṛtāḥ aparvāṇaḥ tu girayaḥ parvabhiḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ śālmaliḥ śālmale dvīpe pūjyate su mahā vrataiḥ kuśadvīpe kuśastaṃbaḥ tasya nāmnā saḥ ucyate śākadvīpe drumaḥ śākaḥ tasya nāmnā saḥ ucyate mahādevaḥ pūjyate tu brahmā tribhuvana īśvaraḥ tasmin vasati brahmā sādhyaiḥ sārddham prajāpatiḥ upāsaṃte tatra devāḥ trayastriṃśat mahā ṛṣibhiḥ dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu prajānām kramatas tu vai ārogya yus pramāṇābhyām pramāṇam dviguṇam tatas gopāyati prajāḥ tatra svayaṃbhūḥ jaḍa paṇḍitāḥ īśvaraḥ brahmā tribhuvana īśvaraḥ sa viṣṇoḥ sacivaḥ devaḥ sa pitā sa pitāmahaḥ ṣaṣ rasam su mahā vīryam bhuñjate tu prajāḥ sadā pareṇa puṣkarasya arddhe āvṛtya avasthitaḥ mahān pareṇa tasya mahatī dṛśyate loka saṃsthitiḥ kāñcanī dviguṇā bhūmiḥ sarvā ahi eka śilā upamā tasya apareṇa śailaḥ ca paryāsāt pasmiṇḍalaḥ prakāśaḥ ca aprakāśaḥ ca lokālokaḥ saḥ ucyate yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśa tasya ucchrayaḥ samṛtaḥ tāvān ca vistaraḥ tasya pṛthivyām kāmagaḥ ca saḥ loka arddhe saṃmitāḥ lokāḥ nirālokāḥ tu bāhyatas ālokāt paratas ca api hi aṇḍam ā vṛtya tiṣṭhati aṇḍasya antaḥ tu ime lokāḥ saptadvīpā ca medinī etāvān eva vijñeyaḥ loka antaḥ ca eva yaḥ paraḥ kuṃbha sthāyī bhavet yāt ṛva pratīcyām diśi candramāḥ āditas śuklapakṣasya vapuḥ ca aṇḍasya tadvidham aṇḍānām īdṛśānām tu koṭyaḥ jñeyāḥ sahasraśas tiryak ūrdhvam adhas vā api kāraṇasya avyaya ātmanaḥ dharaṇaiḥ prākṛtaiḥ tat tat āvṛtam prati saptabhiḥ paraspara āvṛtāḥ sarve utpannāḥ ca parasparam aṇḍasya asya samantāt tu sanniviṣṭaḥ ghana udadhiḥ samantāt tu vanodena dhāryamāṇaḥ sa tiṣṭati dhāryamāṇam samantāt tu tiṣṭhate yat tu tejasā ayaḥ guḍa nibhaḥ vā ahnaḥ samantāt maṇḍala ākṛtiḥ samantāt dhana vātena dhāryamāṇaḥ sa tiṣṭhati ghana vātam tathā ākāśaḥ dadhānaḥ khalu tiṣṭhati bhūtādiḥ ca tathā kāśam bhūtādiḥ ca api asau mahān na eka yojana sāhasram viprakṛṣṭam anāvṛtam ca viśyātam ākāśa ante hi abhāsvaram tridaśānām agamyam tata sthānam divyam iti śrutiḥ candra ādityau adhastāt tu ye lokāḥ prathitāḥ budhaiḥ āpātālāt divam yāvat atra pañcavidhā gatiḥ pramāṇam etat jagataḥ eṣa saṃsāra sāgaraḥ vicitrā jagataḥ sā vai prakṛtiḥ brahmaṇaḥ sthitā pṛthivī aṃbu agni vāyūnām nabhasaḥ tamasaḥ tathā kṣayaḥ vā pariṇāmaḥ vā antaḥ vā api na vidyate anantaḥ eṣa sarvatra evam jñāneṣu paṭhyate tasya ca uktam mayā tasmin nāma anukīrtane yaḥ padmanābha nāmnā tu tad kārtsnyena ca kīrttitaḥ arṇaveṣu ca sarveṣu divi ca eva na saṃśayaḥ anekadhā vibhakta aṅgaḥ mahā yogī janārdanaḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvena vikārāḥ te avikāriṇaḥ yasmāt sṛṣaṭāḥ tu te anyonyam tasmāt sthairyam upāgatāḥ prāk āsanna viśeṣāḥ tu viśeṣaḥ anya viśeṣaṇāt guṇa upacaya sāreṇa paricchedaḥ viśeṣataḥ śeṣāṇām tu paricchedaḥ saukṣmyāt na iha vibhāvyate bhūtebhyaḥ paratas tebhyaḥ vyālokā sā dharā smṛtā bhūtāni āloke ākāśe paricchinnāni sarvaśas pātre mahati pātrāṇi yathā eva antargatāni tu tathā hi āloke ākāśe bhedāḥ tu antargatāḥ matāḥ tantunām iva saṃtāraḥ bhūteṣu antargataḥ mataḥ tasmāt parimitāḥ bhedāḥ smṛtāḥ kāryya ātmakāḥ tu te kāraṇa ātmakāḥ syuḥ bhedāḥ ye mahat ādayaḥ iti eṣa saṃniveśaḥ vai mayā proktaḥ vibhāgaśaḥ sapta dvīpa samudrāḍyaḥ vai dvijāḥ vistarāt maṇḍalāḥ ca eva prasaṃkhyānena ca eva hi vaiśvarū pradhānasya pariṇāma eka deśikaḥ evaṃbhūta gaṇāḥ sapta sanniviṣṭāḥ parasparam etāvān saṃniveśaḥ tu mayā śakyaḥ prabhāṣitum etāvat eva śrotavyam saṃniveśe tu pārtheve tāḥ tu aham parimāṇena nam saṃkhyātum iha utsahe asaṃkhyātāḥ prakṛtayaḥ tiryyak ūrddhvam adhas tathā tārakā saṃniveśaḥ ca yāvat divya anu maṇḍalam paryyāḥ ya sat niveśaḥ tu bhūmeḥ tadanu maṇḍalaḥ atas ūrdhvam pravakṣyāmi kṛthivyāḥ vai vicakṣaṇāḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde plakṣādidvīpavarṇanam nāma ekonaviṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca adhas pramāṇam ūrddhva ca vakṣyamāṇam nibodhata pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam āpaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam anantāḥ dhātavaḥ hi etam vyāpakāḥ tu prakīrttitāḥ jananī sarva bhūtānām sarva sattva dharā dharā nānā janapada ākīrṇā nānā adhiṣṭhāna pattanā nānā nada nadī śailā nā eka jāti samākulā anantā gīyate devī pṛthivī bahu vistarā kṣudra āśraya sthitāḥ parvata ākāśa saṃsthāḥ ca antar bhūmi gātāḥ ca yāḥ āpaḥ anantāḥ hi vijñeyāḥ tathā agniḥ sarva loka gaḥ tathā ākāśam anālekhyam ramyam nānā āśrayam smṛtam anantam paṭhyate ca eva vāyuḥ ca ākāśa sambhavaḥ āpaḥ pṛthivyām udake pṛthivī upari saṃsthitāḥ ākāśaḥ ca aparam atha punar bhūmiḥ punar jalam bhūmiḥ jalam athā kāśam iti yā yā paraṃparā eteṣām api adhobhāge pātālam saptamam smṛtam kṛṣṇabhaumaḥ ca prathamaḥ bhūmi bhāgaḥ prakīrttitaḥ pāṇḍu bhūmiḥ dvitīyaḥ tu tṛtīyaḥ nīlamṛttikaḥ pītabhaumaḥ caturthaḥ tu pañcamaḥ śarkarāmayaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ śilā mayaḥ jñeyaḥ sauvarṇaḥ saptamaḥ smṛtaḥ niṣkulādasya ca puram prahṛṣṭa jana saṃkulam rākṣasasya ca bhīmasya śūla dantasya ca ālayam lohitākṣaka liṅgānām nagaram śvāpadasya ca evam pura sahasrāṇi nāga dānava rakṣasām tale jñeyāni prathame kṛṣṇa bhaume na saṃśayaḥ ālayam kukupādasya mahoṣṇīṣasya ca ālayam evam pura sahasrāṇi nāga dānava rakṣasām dvitīye asmin tale viprāḥ pāṇḍu bhaume na saṃśayaḥ tṛtīye tu tale khyātam prahlādasya mahātmanaḥ tārakāśyasya ca puram puram triśirasaḥ tathā purañjanasya daityasya hṛṣṭa puṣṭa jana ākulam evam pura sahasrāṇi nāga dānava rakṣasām tṛtīye asmin tale viprāḥ nīlabhaume na saṃśayaḥ sahāmeghasya ca puram rākṣasa iṃdrasya mālinaḥ evam pura sahasrāṇi nāga dānava rakṣasām pañcame asmin tale jñeyam śarkarā nicaye sadā rākṣasa iṃdrasya ca puram suroṣasya mahātmanaḥ tatra āste suramā putraḥ śata śīrṣaḥ mudā yutaḥ mahā indrasya sakhā śrīmān vāsuki nāma nāga rāj evam pura sahasrāṇi nāga dānava rakṣasām ṣaṣṭhe tale asmin vikhyāte śilābhaume rasātale puram baleḥ pramuditam rī gaṇa ākulam asura āśīviṣaiḥ pūrṇam sukhitaiḥ deva śatrubhiḥ anekaiḥ diti putrāṇām samudīrṇaiḥ mahā puraiḥ daityānām dānavānām ca samudīrṇaiḥ mahā puraiḥ udīrṇaiḥ rākṣasa āvāsaiḥ anekaiḥ ca samākulam pātāla ante ca vipra indrāḥ bahu yojane āste rakta aravinda akṣaḥ mahātmā hi ajara amaraḥ mahā balaḥ viśāla bhogaḥ dyutimān citra mālya dharaḥ balī rukma śṛṅga avadātena dīpta āsyena virājatā sa jihvā mālayā dīptaḥ lolat jvālā anala arciṣā jvālā mālā parikṣiptaḥ kailāsaḥ iva lakṣya te bāla sūrya abhitāmreṇa śarīra snigdha pāṇḍunā vistīrṇaḥ iva medinyām sahasra śikharaḥ giriḥ mahā nāgaiḥ mahā bhogaiḥ mahā vijñaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ upāsyate mahā tejāḥ mahā nāga patiḥ svayam sa rājā sarva nāgānām śeṣaḥ anantaḥ mahā dyutiḥ sā vaiṣṇavī vyavahṛtiḥ maryādā yā vyavasthitā sapta evam ete kathitāḥ vyavahāryāḥ rasātalāḥ deva asura ma hā nāga rākṣasa adhyuṣitāḥ sadā devānām api a viditam vyavahāra vivakṣayā nabhasaḥ ca dvijottamāḥ mahat tvam ṛṣibhiḥ ca evam varṇyate na atra saṃśayaḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyu prokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde adholokavarṇanam nāma viṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca prakāśaiḥ tu prabhābhiḥ tau maṇḍalābhyām samucchritau saptānām tu samudrāṇām dvīpānām satu vistaraḥ paryāsa parimāṇam tu candra ādityau prakāśataḥ paryāstāt pārimāṇyena bhūmeḥ tulyam divam smṛtam avati trīn imān lokān yasmāt sūryaḥ paribhraman avidhātuḥ prakāśa ākhyaḥ hi avanāt sa raviḥ smṛtaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi pramāṇam candra sūryayoḥ maṇḍalam bhāskarasya atha yojanāni nibodhata vistārāt triguṇaḥ ca asya pariṇāhaḥ tu maṇḍale viṣkaṃbha maṇḍalāt ca eva bhāskarāt dviguṇaḥ śaśī atha pṛthivyāḥ vakṣyāmi pramāṇam yojanaiḥ saha sapta dvīpa samudrāyāḥ vistāraḥ maṇḍalam ca yat iti etat iha saṃkhyātam purāṇe parimāṇataḥ tat vakṣyāmi samākhyāya sāṃprataiḥ abhimānibhiḥ divā astu sanniveśam vai sāṃprataiḥ eva kṛtsnaśas śata arddha koṭi vistārā pṛthivī kṛtsnaśas smṛtā tasyāḥ ūrddhva pramāṇena meroḥ yāvat tu saṃsthitiḥ pṛthivyāḥ hi arddha vistāraḥ yojana agrāt prakīrttitaḥ meroḥ madhyāt pratidiśam koṭiḥ ekā tu sā smṛtā tathā śāta sahasrāṇām ekona navatiḥ punar pañcāśat tu sahasrāṇi pṛthivī arddhasya maṇḍalam gaṇitam yojana agrāt tu koṭyaḥ tu ekādaśa smṛtāḥ tathā śata sahasrāṇi saptatriṃśa adhikāni tu iti etat iha saṃśyātam pṛthivī antasya maṇḍalam tārakā saṃniveśā asya divi yāva ca maṇḍalam paryāsa sanniveśaḥ ca bhūmeḥ yāvat tu maṇḍalam paryāsa parimāṇena bhūmeḥ tulyam divaḥ smṛtam saptānām api dvīpānām etat tsthānam prakīrtitam paryāya parimāṇena maṇḍala anugatena ca saṃsthitiḥ vihitā sarvā yeṣu tiṣṭhanti jantavaḥ etat aṇḍa kapālasya pramāṇam parikīrttitam aṇḍasya antaḥ tu ime lokāḥ saptadvīpā ca medinī ete sapta kṛtāḥ lokāḥ chatra ākārāḥ vyavasthitāḥ svakaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ dhāryamāṇāḥ pṛthak pṛthak daśa bhāga adhikābhiḥ ca tābhiḥ prakṛtibhiḥ bahis pūryamāṇāḥ viśeṣaiḥ ca samutpannaiḥ parasparāt asya aṇḍasya samantāt ca sanniviṣṭaḥ ghana udadhiḥ pṛthivyāḥ maṇḍalam kṛtsnam ghana toyena dhāryate saṃmatāt dhana vātena dhāryamāṇam pratiṣṭhitam ghana vātam tathā ākāśam ākāśam ca mahātmanā bhūtādinā vṛtam sarvam bhūtādiḥ mahatā vṛtaḥ vṛtaḥ mahān anantena yā ātmanā purāṇi lokapālānām pravakṣyāmi yathākramam meroḥ prācyām diśi tathā mānasasya eva mūrddhani vasvaukasārā māhendrī purī hema pariṣkṛtā sukhā nāma purī ramyā varuṇasya api dhīmataḥ varuṇaḥ yādasām nāthaḥ sukha ākhye vasate pure mānasa uttara vṛṣṭe tu lokapālāḥ caturdiśam lokapāla upariṣṭāt tu sarvatas dakṣiṇāyane kāṣṭhā gatasya sūryasya gatiyā tām nibodhata dakṣiṇaḥ apakrame sūryaḥ kṣipta iṣuḥ iva sarpati jyotiṣām cakram ādāya satatam parigacchati madhya gaḥ ca amarāvatyām yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ sukhāyām arddharātram syāt vibhāyām astam eti ca sukhāyām atha vāruṇyām uttiṣṭhan sa tu dṛśyate vibhāyāḥ mā ṛddharātram syāt māhendyām astam eti ca yadā aparāhṇaḥ vidhīyate dakṣiṇa apara deśyānām pūrva hṇaḥ parikī rttitaḥ teṣām apararātraḥ ca ye janāḥ uttarāḥ pare deśāḥ uttara pūrvāḥ ye pūvarātraḥ tu tān prati sukhāyāsatha vāruṇyām madhyāhne ca aryamā yadā vibhāyām soma puryām vai uttiṣṭhati vibhāvasuḥ somapuryāḥ vibhāyām tu madhyāhne syāt divākaraḥ mahedrasya amarāvatyām sūryaḥ uttiṣṭhate tadā arddharātram saṃyamane vāruṇyām astam eti ca bhraman vai bhramamā arṇāni ṛkṣāṇi carate raviḥ evam caturṣu pārśveṣu dakṣiṇām tena sarpati udaya astamane ca asau ṛtti ṣṭhati punar punar pūvāhṇe ca aparāhṇe ca dvau dvau devālayau tu saḥ udaya astamayābhyām ca smṛte pūrva apare diśau yāvat purastāt tapati tāpat pṛṣṭhe atha pārśvayoḥ yatra udyan dṛśyate sūryaḥ teṣām saḥ udayaḥ samṛtaḥ praṇāśam gacchate yatra teṣām astaḥ saḥ ucyate sarveṣām uttare meruloṅkālokaḥ ca dakṣiṇe vidūra bhāvāt arkasya bhūmi lekhā vṛtasya ca līyante raśmayaḥ yasmāt tena rātrau na dṛśyate graha nakṣatra somānām darśanam bhāskarasya ca śukla chāyaḥ agniḥ ā paśca kṛṣṇa chāyā ca medinī rakta bhāvaḥ viraśma tvāt rakta tvāt jā api anuṣṇa tā lekhāyām āsthitaḥ sūryaḥ yatra yatra ca dṛśyate ūrddhva tu yojanānām sa dṛśyate agnim āviśate rādrau tasmāt dūrāt prakāśate udite hi punar sūrye hi auṣṇyam āgneyam āviśet prākāśyam ca tathā auṣṇyam ca saura āgneye ca tejasī paraspara anupraveśāt dīpyete tu divāniśam uttiṣṭhati tathā sūrye rātriḥ āviśata tvapaḥ tasmāt śītāḥ bhaktyā aṃpaḥ divā rātri praveśanāt astam yāti punar sūrye dinam āviśate tvaṣaḥ tasmāt uṣṇāḥ bhavati āpaḥ naktam ahnaḥ praveśanāt sūrya prakāśa ākhyam tāmasī rātriḥ ūcyate tasmāt vyavasthitā rātriḥ sūrya apekṣam ahar smṛtam aṃśa aṃśakam tu medinyām muhūrttena eva gacchati pūrṇe śata sahasrāṇām ekatriṃśa adhikam smṛtam pañcāśat tu tathā anyāni sahasrāṇi adhikāni ca mauhūrtti kī gatiḥ hi eṣā sūryasya tu vidhīyate etena gati yogena yadā kāṣṭhām tu dakṣiṇām sarpate dakṣiṇāyām tu kāṣṭhāyām vai nibodhata nava koṭyaḥ prasaṃkhyātāḥ yojanaiḥ parimaṇḍalam tathā śata sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśat ca pañca ca ahorātrāt pataṅgasya gatiḥ eṣā vidhīyate dakṣiṇāt vinivṛttaḥ asau viṣuva sthaḥ yadā raviḥ tisraḥ koṭyaḥ tu saṃkhyātāḥ viṣuvasya api maṇḍalam tathā śata sahasrāṇām aśīti eka adhikā punar śravaṇe ca uttaraṣāḍhe citrabhānuḥ yadā bhavet śākadvīpasya ṣaṣṭhasya uttarātas diśaḥ caran utarāyāḥ pramāṇam ca kāṣṭhāyāḥ maṇḍalasya ca yojana agrāt prasaṃkhyātā koṭiḥ ekā tu sa dvijāḥ aśītiḥ niyutāni iha yojanānām tathā eva ca aṣṭapañcāśatam yojanāni adhikāni tu nāgavīthī uttarāvīthī hi aja vīthī ca dakṣiṇā mūlam ca eva tathā āṣāḍhe tu ajavīthī udayāḥ trayaḥ aśvinī kṛttikā yāmyam nāgavīthī udayāḥ trayaḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ antaram yat ca tat vakṣyeya janaiḥ punar etat śata sahasrāṇām aṣṭābhiḥ ca uttaram śatam trayaḥ śata adhikāḥ ca nye trayastriṃśat ca yojanaiḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ antaram hi etat yojana agrāt prakīrtitam kāṣṭhayoḥ lekhayoḥ ca eva hi antaram dakṣiṇa uttare sahasrāṇi atiriktāḥ ca tatas anyā pañcasaptatiḥ lekhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ ca eva bāhya abhyantarayoḥ smṛtam abhyantaram tu paryeti maṇḍalāni uttarāyaṇe maṇḍalānām śatam pūrmam tri aśīti adhikam uttaram carate dakṣiṇe ca api tāvat eva vibhāvasuḥ pramāṇam maṇḍalasya atha yojana agram nibodhata yojanānām sahasrāṇi saptādaśa samāsatas etat pramāṇam ākhyātam yojanaiḥ maṇḍalasya ca pratyaham carate tāni sūryāḥ vai maṇḍala kramāt dakṣiṇa prakrame sūryaḥ tathā śīghram pravarttate tasmāt prakṛṣṭām bhūmim tu kālena alpena gacchati sūryaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ śairghyāt muhūrtaiḥ dakṣiṇāyane trayodaśa arddham ṛkṣāṇām ahnā tu carate raviḥ muhūrtaiḥ stāvat ṛkṣāṇi naktam aṣṭādaśaiḥ caran aṣṭādaśa muhūrta tu uttarāyaṇapaścimam trayodaśa arddham mādyena tu ṛkṣāṇām carate raviḥ muhūrtaiḥ tāvat ṛkṣāṇi naktam dvādaśabhiḥ caran triṃśat muhūrtān eva āhuḥ ahorātram dhruvaḥ bhraman ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ madhye bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoḥ madhye bhramate maṇḍalāni saḥ divānaktam ca sūryasya mandā śīghrā ca vai gātiḥ tathā eva ca punar naktam śīghrā sūryasya vai gātiḥ dakṣiṇa prakrameṇa eva divā śīghram vidhīyate evam gati viśeṣeṇa vibhajan rātri ahāni tu saṃcaran mārgam samena viṣameṇa ca lokāloka sthitāḥ hi ete lokapālāḥ caturdiśam agastyaḥ carate teṣām upariṣṭāt javena tu bhuñjan asāpahorā tram evam gati viśeṣaṇam dakṣiṇe nāgavīthyāḥ tu lokālokasya ca uttare loka santānakaḥ hi eṣa vaiśvānara pathāt vahis pṛṣṭe yāvat prabhā saurī purastāt saṃprakāśate pārśvatas pṛṣṭhatas ca eva lokālokasya varttate yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśakam tucchritaḥ giriḥ prakāśaḥ ca aprakāśaḥ ca sarvatas parimaṇḍalaḥ nakṣatra candra sūryaḥ ca grahaiḥ tārā gaṇaiḥ saha tasmāt sandhyā iti tām āhuḥ uṣā vyuṣṭyoḥ yat antaram uṣāḥ rātriḥ smṛtā vipraiḥ vyuṣṭiḥ ca api tu ahar smṛtam sūrya agni grasamānānām saṃdhyā kāle hi rakṣasām prajāpati niyogena śāpaḥ tu eṣām durātmanām akṣaya tvam tu dehasya prāpita āmraṇam tathā tisraḥ koṭyaḥ tu vikhyātāḥ mandehāḥ nāma rākṣasāḥ tāpayantam durātmānaḥ sūryam icchanti khāditum atha sūryasya teṣām ca yuddham āsīt su dāruṇam tatas brahmā ca devāḥ ca brāhmamāḥ ca eva sattamāḥ saṃdhyām tu samupāsīnāḥ prakṣipanti jalam sadā oṅkāra brahma saṃyuktam gāyatryā ca abhimantritam sphūrjat jyotiḥ ca caṇḍāṃśuḥ tathā dīpyati bhāskaraḥ tatas punar mahā tejāḥ mahā bala parākramaḥ yojanānām sahasrāṇi ūrddhvam uttiṣṭhate śatam prayāti bhagavān āśu brāhmaṇaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ vālakhilyaiḥ ca munibhiḥ dhṛta arciḥ sa marīcibhiḥ kāṣṭhāḥ nimeṣāḥ daśa pañca ca eva triṃśat ca kāṣṭhāḥ gaṇayet kalām tu triṃśat kalāḥ ca api bhavet muhūrttaḥ taiḥ triṃśatā rātri ahanī samete hrāsa vṛddhī tu ahar bhāgaiḥ divasānām yathākramāt saṃdhyā muhūrtta mātrā tu hrāsa vṛddhiḥ tu sā smṛtā prātar tatas smṛtaḥ kālaḥ bhāgaḥ ca ahnaḥ sa pañcamaḥ tasmāt prātastanāt kālāt ri muhūrttaḥ tu saṃgavaḥ madhyāhnaḥ tri muhūrttaḥ tu tasmāt kālaḥ ca saṃgavāt tasmāt madhyandināt kālāt aparāhṇaḥ iti smṛtaḥ trayaḥ eva muhūrttāḥ tu kālāgaḥ smṛtaḥ budhaiḥ aparāhṇe vyatīte tu kālaḥ sāyāhnaḥ ucyate daśa pañca muhūrta ahnaḥ muhūrttāḥ trayaḥ eva ca ahorātre kalāḥ ca eva samam somaḥ samaśnute tathā pañcadaśa ahāni pakṣaḥ iti abhidhīyate dvau ca pakṣau bhavet māsaḥ dvau māsau arka jau ṛtuḥ nimeṣāḥ vidyutaḥ ca eva kāṣṭāḥ tāḥ daśa pañca ca kalāḥ tāḥ triśataḥ kāṣṭhā mātrā śīti dvaya ātmikā sapta ekā dvi adhikā triśat mātrā ṣaṭatriṃśat uttarā dviṣā aṣṭinā trayoviṃśat mātrāyāḥ ca kalā bhavet catvāri śat sahasrāṇi śatāni aṣṭau ca vidyutaḥ varāṃśaḥ hi eṣa vijñeyaḥ nāḍikā ca atra kāraṇam saṃvatsara ādayaḥ pañca catur māna vikalpitāḥ iḍā vatsaraḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu caturthaḥ ca anuvatsaraḥ pañcamaḥ vatsaraḥ teṣām kālaḥ tu yuga saṃhitaḥ triṃśat śatam bhavet pūrṇam parvaṇām tu raveḥ yuge śatāni aṣṭādaśa triṃśat udayāt bhāskarasya ca ṛtavaḥ triṃśataḥ saurāt ayanāni daśa eva tu pañca ca tri śatam ca api ṣaṣṭi varṣam ca bhāskaram ekaṣaṣṭi tu ahorātram ṛtuḥ ekaḥ vibhāvyate ahnām tu tri adhika aśītiḥ śatam ca api adhikam bhavet sauram saumyam tu vijñeyam nākṣatram sāvanam tathā mānāni etāni catvāri yaiḥ purāṇe hi niścayaḥ yaḥ śvetasya uttaraḥ ca eva śṛṅgavān nāma parvvataḥ trīṇi tasya tu śṛṅgāṇi spṛśanti iva nabhastalam taiḥ ca api śṛṅgaiḥ sa nagaḥ śṛṅgavān n iti kathyate ekaḥ ca mārga viṣkaṃbha vistāraḥ ca asya kīrtitaḥ tasya vai pūrvatas śṛṅgam madhyamam tat hiraṇmayam dakṣiṇam rājatam ca eva śṛṅgam tu sphaṭika prabham evam kūṭaiḥ tribhiḥ śailaḥ śṛṅgavān iti viśrutaḥ yat tat vai pūrvatas śṛṅgam tat arkaḥ pratipadyate haritāḥ ca hayāḥ divyāḥ tasya yuktāḥ mahā rathe ca tulā ante ca bhāskara udayataḥ smṛtāḥ muhūrttāḥ daśa pañca eva ahaḥ rātriḥ ca tāvatī kṛttikānām yadā sūryaḥ prathamām śa gataḥ bhavet viśākhānām tadā jñeyaḥ caturtha aṃśa niśākaraḥ viśākhānām yadā sūryaḥ carata iṃśam tṛtīyakam tadā candram vijānīyāt kṛttikā śirasi sthitam viṣuvam tam vijānīyāt evam āhuḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ sūryeṇa viṣuvam vidyāt kālam somena lakṣayet samāḥ rātriḥ ahar ca eva yadā tat viṣuvam bhavet tadā dānāni deyāni pitṛbhyaḥ viṣuveṣu ca ūna māsa adhimāsau ca kalā kāṣṭhā muhūrttakāḥ paurṇamāsī tathā jñeyā amāvāsyā tathā eva ca sinīvālī kuhūḥ ca eva rākā ca anumatiḥ tathā nabhaḥ nabhasya viṣa ūrja saṃjñau sahaḥ sahasyau iti dakṣiṇam syāt ārtavāḥ ca tatas jñeyā pañca abdāḥ brahmaṇāḥ sutāḥ tasmāt ca ṛtavaḥ jñeyāḥ ṛtubhyaḥ hi ārttavāḥ smṛtāḥ tasmāt ṛtu mukhī jñeyā amāvāsyā asya parvaṇaḥ tasmāt tu viṣuvam jñeyam pitṛ deva hitam sadā tasmāt smṛtam pracānām vai viṣuvat sarva gam sadā catvāraḥ te mahātmānaḥ tiṣṭanti ā bhūta saṃplavāt sudhāmā ca eva vairājaḥ kardamaḥ śaṅkhapāḥ tathā hiraṇya romā parjanyaḥ ketumān rājasaḥ ca yaḥ nirdvandvāḥ nirabhīmānāḥ niḥ sīmāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ lokapālāḥ sthitāḥ hi ete lokāloke caturdiśam uttaram yat apaḥ tasya hi aja vīthyāḥ ca dakṣiṇām pitṛyānaḥ sa vai panthāḥ vaiśvānara pathāt vahis lokasya saṃtāna karāḥ pitṛ yāna pathe sthitāḥ bhūta āraṃbha kṛtam karma āśiṣaḥ ṛtvij udyatāḥ prārabhante loka kāmāḥ teṣām panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇāḥ saṃtaptāḥ tapasā ca eva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca jāyamānāḥ tu pūrve vai paścimānām gṛhe su iha paścimāḥ ca eva pūrveṣām jāyante nidhaneṣu api evam āvarttamānāḥ te tiṣṭhanti ā bhūtasaṃplavāt aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi savituḥ dakṣiṇam mārga śritāḥ hi ācandratārakam kriyāvatām prasaṃkhyā eṣā ye śmaśānāni bhejire loka saṃvyavahārāḥ ca bhūta āraṃbha kṛtena ca etaiḥ taiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhāḥ ye śmaśānāni bhejire nāgavīthī uttaraḥ yaḥ ca saptarṣi gaṇa dakṣiṇaḥ uttaraḥ savituḥ panthāḥ deva yānaḥ ca sa smṛtaḥ yatra te vāsinaḥ siddhāḥ vimalāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇām ūrddhvaretasām udak panthānam atyartham śritāḥ hi āśrita saṃplavāt icchā dveṣa nivṛttyā ca bhūta āraṃbha vivarjanāt punar ca a kāma saṃyogāt śabda ādeḥ deṣadar śanāt iti etaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhāḥ te amṛta tvam hi bhejire ābhūtasaṃplava sthānām amṛta tvam vibhāvyate brūṇahatyā aśvamedhābhyām puṇya pāpa kṛtaḥ apare ā bhūta saṃplava ante tu kṣīyam te hi ūrdhvaretasaḥ etat viṣṇu padam divyam tṛtīyam vyomni bhāsvaram yatra gatvā na śocanti tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam dharma dhruva ādyāḥ tiṣṭhanti yatra te loka sādhakāḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde ādityavyūhakīrttanam nāma ekaviṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca svāyaṃbhūva nisarge tu vyākhyātāni antarāṇi ca bhaviṣyāṇi ca sarvāṇi teṣām vakṣyāmi anukramam sūryācandramasoḥ cāram grahāṇām ca eva sarvaśas ṛṣayaḥ ṛcuḥ avyūhena ca sarvāṇi tathā eva asaṃkareṇa vā sūtaḥ uvāca pratyakṣam api dṛśyam ca saṃmohayati yat prajāḥ yaḥ ayam caturddiśam pucche śaiśumāre vyavasthitaḥ dhruvasya manasā ca asau sarvate jyotiṣām gaṇaḥ sūryācandramasau tārāḥ nakṣatrāṇi grahaiḥ saha teṣām yogaḥ ca bhedaḥ ca kālaḥ cāraḥ tathā eva ca varṣāḥ gharmaḥ himam rātriḥ saṃdhyā ca eva dinam tathā śubha aśubham prajānām ca dhruvāt sarvam pravarttate dhruveṇa adhiṣṭitaḥ ca eva sūryaḥ apaḥ gṛhya varṣati tat eṣa dīpta kiraṇaḥ sa kālagniḥ divākaraḥ sūryaḥ kirama jālena vāyu yuktena sarvaśas āditya pītam sakalam somaḥ saṃkramate jalam nāḍībhiḥ vāyu yuktābhiḥ loka dhārā pravarttate meghāḥ vāyu vighātena visṛjanti jalam bhūvi saṃdhāraṇa artham lokānām māyā eṣā viśva nirmitā anyā māyayā vyāptam trailokyam sacarācaram viśveśaḥ loka kṛt devaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ dhātā kṛtsnasya lokasya prabhaviṣṇuḥ divākaraḥ sūryāt uṣṇam nisravate somāt śītam pravarttate śīta uṣṇa vīryauṃ dvau etau yuktyā dhārayataḥ jagat somādhārā nadī gaṅgā pavitrā vimala udakā sarva bhūta śarīreṣu hi āpaḥ hi anusṛtāḥ ca yāḥ teṣu saṃdahyamāneṣu jaṅgama sthāvareṣu ca dhūma bhūtāḥ tu tāḥ hi āpaḥ niṣkāmanti iha sarvaśas tena ca abhrāṇi jāyante sthānam abhra mayam smṛtam saṃjīvanam ca sasyānām aṃbhaḥ tat amṛta upamam tatas tu ṛtu vaśāt kāle parivatya divākaraḥ abhra sthāḥ prapatanti āpaḥ vāyunā samudīritāḥ sarva bhūta hita arthāya vāyu miśrāḥ samantataḥ tatas varṣati ṣaṣ māsān sarva bhūta vivṛddhaye āgneyāḥ brahma jāḥ ca eva pakṣajāḥ ca pṛthagvidhāḥ tridhā meghāḥ samākhyātāḥ teṣām vakṣyāmi saṃbhavam āgneyāḥ stu uṣṇajāḥ proktāḥ teṣām dhūma pravarttanam śīta durdina vātāḥ ye sva guṇāḥ te vyavasthitāḥ mahiṣāḥ ca vārāhāḥ ca matta mātaṅga rūpiṇaḥ jīmūtāḥ nāma te meghāḥ hi etebhyaḥ jīva saṃbhavaḥ vidyut guṇa vihīnāḥ ca jala dhārāḥ vilaṃbinaḥ mūka meghāḥ mahā kāyāḥ āvahasya vaśa anugāḥ krośa mātrāt ca varṣanti krośa arddhāt api vā punar balākā garbha dāḥ ca eva balākā garbha dhāriṇaḥ brahmajāḥ nāma te meghāḥ brahma niśvāsa saṃbhavāḥ teṣām śaśrvat praṇādena bhūmiḥ sva aṅgarūha udbhavā rājñī rājya abhiṣiktā iva punar yauṃvanam aśnute teṣu iyam prāvṛṣ āsaktā bhūtānām jīvita udbhavā dvitīyam pravaham vāyum meghāḥ te tu samāśritāḥ etam yojana mātrāt ca sādhya ṛddhā niṣkṛtāt api vṛṣṭiḥ garbhaḥ tridhā teṣām dhārā sāraḥ prakīrttitaḥ puṣkarāvarttakāḥ nāma te meghāḥ pakṣa saṃbhavāḥ śakreṇa pakṣa chinnāḥ ye parvatānām mahā ojasām pravṛddhānām bhūtānām śivam icchatā puṣkarāḥ nāma te meghāḥ bṛṃhantaḥ toya matsarāḥ puṣkarāvarttakāḥ tena kāraṇena iha śabditāḥ nānā rūpa dharāḥ ca eva mahā ghora svanāḥ ca te kalpānta vṛṣṭeḥ sraṣṭāraḥ saṃvarta agneḥ niyāmakāḥ varṣanti ete yuga anteṣu tṛtīyāḥ te prakīrttitāḥ aneka rūpa saṃsthānāḥ pūrayantaḥ mahī talam vāyum purā vahantaḥ syuḥ āśritāḥ kalpa sādhakāḥ yāni aṇḍasya tu bhinnasya prākṛtasya abhavan tadā tāni eva aṇḍa kapālāni sarve meghāḥ prakīrttitāḥ teṣām āpyāyanam dhūmaḥ sarveṣām aviśeṣatas teṣām śreṣṭhaḥ tu parjanyaḥ catvāraḥ ca eva diggajāḥ gajānām parvatānām ca meghānām bhogibhiḥ saha kulam ekam pṛthak bhūtam yoniḥ ekā jalam smṛtam parjanyaḥ diggajāḥ ca eva hemante śīta saṃbhavāḥ tuṣāra vṛṣṭim varṣanti śiṣṭaḥ sasya pravṛddhaye ṣaṣṭhaḥ parivahaḥ nāma teṣām vāyuḥ apāśrayaḥ yaḥ asau bibartti bhagavān gaṅgām ākāśa gocarām divya amṛta jalā puṇyām tridhā svāti pathe sthitām tasyāḥ nisyanda toyāni diggajāḥ pṛthubhiḥ karaiḥ śīkaram saṃpramuñcanti nīhāraḥ iti sa smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇena giriḥ yaḥ asau hemakūṭaḥ iti smṛtaḥ puṇḍram nāma samākhyātam nagaram tatra vistṛtam himavantam atikramya vṛṣṭi śeṣam tatas param iha abhyeti tatas paścāt apara anta vivṛddhaye sūryaḥ eva tu vṛṣṭīnām sraṣṭā samupadiśyate sūrya mūlā ca vai vṛṣṭiḥ jalam sūryāt pravartate dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitaḥ sūryaḥ tasyām vṛṣṭau pravarttate dhruveṇa adhiṣṭitaḥ vāyuḥ vṛṣṭim saṃharate punar grahaḥ niḥsṛtya sūryāt tu kṛtsne nakṣatra maṇḍale caritvā ante viśati arkam dhruveṇa samādhiṣṭhitam saṃsthitena eka cakreṇa pañca āreṇa tri nābhinā aṣṭāpada nibaddhena ṣaṣ prakāra eka neminā daśa yojana sāhasraḥ vistāra āyāmataḥ smṛtaḥ dviguṇaḥ asya rathopasthāt īṣā daṇḍaḥ pramāṇataḥ sa tasya brahmaṇā sṛṣṭaḥ rathaḥ hi artha vaśena tu vāruṇa syandanasya iha lakṣaṇaiḥ sadṛśaḥ tu saḥ arāḥ pañca ārttavān tasya nemiḥ ṣaṣ ṛtavaḥ smṛtaḥ rathanīḍaḥ smṛtaḥ hi eṣa ca ayane kūbarau ubhau muhūrttāḥ bandhurāḥ tasya ramyāḥ ca asya kalāḥ smṛtāḥ tasya kāṣṭhā smṛtā ghoṇā akṣa daṇḍaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tu vai nimeṣaḥ ca anukarṣaḥ asya hi īṣā ca asya lavāḥ smṛtāḥ yuga akṣa koḍī te tasya artha kāmau ubhau smṛtau sapta aśva rūpāḥ chandāsi vahantaḥ vāmatas dhuram gāyatrī ca eva hi anuṣṭubh jagatī tathā paṅktiḥ ca bṛhatī ca eva hi uṣṇih ca eva tu saptamī yuga akṣa koṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya hi hrasataḥ tasya raśmī tu maṇḍaleṣu uttarāyaṇe ākṛṣyete yadā tau vai dhruveṇa sama dhiṣṭhitau aśītiḥ maṇḍala śatam kāṣṭhayoḥ antaram smṛtam dhruveṇa mucyamānābhyām raśmibhyām punar eva tu tathā eva bāhyatas sūryaḥ bhramate maṇḍalāni tu udveṣāṭayan sa vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde devagrahānukīrtanam nāma dvāviṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca gandharvaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca grāmaṇīsarpa rākṣasaiḥ dhātā arayamā pulastyaḥ ca pulahaḥ ca prajāpatiḥ erāvataḥ vāsukiḥ ca kaṃsaḥ bhīmaḥ ca tau ubhau rathakṛt ca rathaujāḥ ca yakṣau etau udā tdṛtau rakṣaḥ hetiḥ prahetiḥ ca yātudhānau udāhṛtau mitraḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca eva muniḥ atriḥ udāhṛtaḥ tathā vasiṣṭhaḥ vikhyātaḥ sahajanyā ca menakā hāhā hūhūḥ ca gandharvaum yajñaḥ ca api rathasvanaḥ rathacitraḥ tathā evā anyaḥ nāgasākṣaka saṃjñā itas raṃbhakaḥ ca vasanti ete māsayoḥ śuci śukrayoḥ tatas sūrye punar tu anyāḥ nivasaṃti iha devatāḥ idraḥ ca eva vivasvān ca aṅgirāḥ bhṛguḥ eva ca elāpatraḥ tathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālāḥ ca tau ubhau viśvāvasu ugrasenau ca śvetaḥ ca eva aruṇaḥ tathā śaradi anyāḥ punar śubhrāḥ vasaṃti muni devatāḥ parjanyaḥ ca eva pūṣā ca bhāradvājaḥ sa gautamaḥ viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te śubha lakṣaṇe nāgaḥ erāvataḥ ca eva viśrutaḥ ca dhanañjayaḥ ścenajit ca suṣeṇaḥ ca senīḥ grāma ṇīḥ ca tau āpaḥ vātaḥ ca dvau etau yātudhānau udāhṛtau aṃśaḥ bhagaḥ ca dvau aitau kaśyapaśya kratuḥ ca ha bhujaṅgaḥ ca mahāpadmaḥ sarvaḥ karkeṭakaḥ tathā urvaśī pūrvacittiḥ ca tathā eva apsarasau ubhe tārkṣaḥ ca ariṣṭanemiḥ ca senānīḥ grāmaṇīḥ ca tau vidyut sphūrjaḥ śatāyuḥ ca yātudhānau udātt ṛtau tatas śaiśira yoḥ ca api māsayoḥ nivasaṃti vai tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ jāmadagnyaḥ viśvāmitraḥ tathā eva ca kādraveyau tathā nāgau kaṃbala aśvatarau ubhau gandharvaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ca sūryavarcāḥ tathā eva ca tilottamā tathā raṃbhā brahmāpetaḥ ca rākṣasaḥ yajñāpetam tathā eva anyaḥ viśyātaḥ rākṣasaḥ uttamaḥ pitṛ deva manuṣya ādīn sa sadā āpyāyayan prabhuḥ parivarttati ahorātra kāraṇam savitā dvijāḥ sthāna abhimāninaḥ hi ete gāṇāḥ dvādaśa saptakāḥ kurvate abhīṣu saṃgraham sarpāḥ vahanti vai sūryam yātudhānāḥ tu yānti ca eteṣām eva devānām yathāvīryam yathā tapaḥ yathādharmam yathāyogam yathāsatyam yathābalam tapati asau taśrā sūryaḥ eṣām indraḥ tu tejasā ṛṣayaḥ deva gandharvāḥ pannaga apsarasām gaṇāḥ grāmaṇyaḥ ca tathā yakṣāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca mukhyaśas bhūtānām ca śubham karma vyapohanti prakīrttitāḥ mānavānām śubham hi ete harante durita ātmanām ete saha eva sūryeṇa bhramanti divāsānugāḥ varṣantaḥ ca tapantaḥ ca hlādayantaḥ ca vai prajāḥ gopāyanti ca bhūtāni sarvāṇi īhām anu kṣayāt sthāna abhimāninām etat sthānam manvantareṣu vai atīta anāgatānām ca varttante sāṃpratam ca ye grīṣme ca varṣāsu ca muñcamānaḥ gharmam himam varṣa dinam niśām ca gacchati asau ṛtu vaśāt parivṛtta raśmiḥ devān pitṝn ca manujān ca hi tarpayan vai prīṇāti devān amṛtena sūryaḥ somam suṣumṇena ca varddhayitvā śukle tu pūrṇam divasa krameṇa tam kṛṣṇa pakṣe vibudhāḥ pibanti pītam ca somam hi kalā avaśiṣṭam kṛṣṇa kṣaye raśmibhiḥ akṣarantam sudhā amṛtam tat pitaraḥ pibanti devāḥ ca saumyāḥ ca tathā eva kāvyāḥ sūryeṇa gobhiḥ ca samujjhitābhiḥ adbhiḥ punar ca eva samuddhṛtābhiḥ vṛṣṭyā abhivṛddhābhiḥ atha auṣadhībhiḥ martyāḥ kṣudham tu anna pānaiḥ jayanti tṛptiḥ ca śukle sudhayā surāṇām pakṣe ca kṛṣṇe sudhayā pitaṇām visarga kāle visṛjan ca tāḥ punar bibhartti śaśvat savitā carācaram tryaśīti maṇḍala śatam bhramanti abdena te hayāḥ bāhyam ābhyantaram ca eva maṇḍalam divasa kramāt kalpa ādau saṃpra yuktāḥ te vahanti ā bhūta saṃplavāt sevyate gīta nṛtyaiḥ ca gandharvaiḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ vīthi āśrayāṇi ṛkṣāṇi dhruva ādhāreṇa vegitāḥ hrāsa vṛddhī tathā eva asya raśmīnām sūrya vat smṛte tri cakra ubhayatas aśvaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ śaśinaḥ rathaḥ apām garṇāt samutpannaḥ rathaḥ sa aśvaḥ sa sārathiḥ saṃgṛhīta rathe tasmin śvetaḥ cakṣuḥśravāḥ ca vai aśvāḥ tam eka varṇaḥ te vahante śaṅkha varcasaḥ yajuḥ caṇḍamanāḥ ca eva vṛṣaḥ vājī naraḥ hayaḥ aśvaḥ gaviṣṇuḥ vikhyātaḥ haṃsaḥ vyomaḥ mṛgaḥ tathā devaiḥ pīta tanum somam āpyāyayati nityadā kṣīṇam pañcadaśa aham tu raśminā ekena bhāskaraḥ āpūrayan suṣumṇena bhāgam bhāgam ahar kramāt suṣumṇā āpyāyamānasya śuklāḥ varddhanti vai kalāḥ tasmāt hrasaṃti vai kṛṣṇe śukle su āpyāyayanti tam iti evam sūrya vīryeṇa candraḥ ca āpyāyitaḥ tatas paurṇamāsyām sa dṛśyeta śuklaḥ saṃpūrṇa maṇḍalaḥ evam āpyāyitaḥ somaḥ śukla pakṣe dina kramāt pibati aṃbu mayam devāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ saumyam svadhā amṛtam saṃbhṛtam tu arddha māsena hi amṛtam sūrya tejasā bhakṣa artham amṛtam somaḥ paurṇamāsyām upāsate ekām rātrim suraiḥ sarvaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ sa ṛṣibhiḥ saha somasya kṛṣṇa pakṣa ādau bhāskara abhimukhasya tu prakṣīyante pidṛdevaiḥ pīyamānāḥ kalāḥ kramāt iti etaiḥ pīyamānasya kṛṣṇāḥ varddhati vai kalāḥ kṣīyanti tasmāt śuklāḥ ca kṛṣṇāḥ āpyāyayanti ca pītvā arddha māsam gacchanti ca amāvāsyām sura uttamāḥ pitaraḥ ca upatiṣṭhanti hi amāvāsyām niśākaram tatas pañcadaśe kāle kiñcid śiṣṭe kalā ātmake aparāhṇe pitṛ gaṇāḥ jaghanyam payu upāsate pibanti dvi lavam kālam śiṣṭāḥ tasya kalāḥ tu yāḥ niḥsṛtam tat amāvāsyām gabhastibhyaḥ svadhā amṛtam tām svadhām māsa tṛptyai ca pītvā gacchanti te amṛtam kṛṣṇa pakṣe suraiḥ tadvat pīyate vai sudhā mayaḥ saumyāḥ barhiṣadaḥ ca eva agniṣvāttāḥ ca te tridhā saṃvatsarāḥ tu vai kāvyāḥ pañca abdāḥ ye dvicaiḥ smṛtāḥ saumyāḥ tu jñeyāḥ māsāḥ barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ agniṣvātta ārttavāḥ ca eva pitṛ sargāḥ hi vai dvijāḥ pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānasya pañcadaśyām kalā tu vai yāvat prakṣīyate tasya bhāgaḥ pañcadaśaḥ tu yaḥ amāvāsyām tadā tasya tatas āpūryate paraḥ vṛddha kṣayau vai pakṣa ādau ṣoḍaśyām śaśinaḥ smṛtā evam sūrya nimittā eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛddhiḥ niśākare tārā grahāṇām vakṣyāmi svarbhānoḥ ca rathān punar bhārgavasya rathaḥ śrīmān tejasā sūrya sannibhaḥ pṛthivī saṃbhavaiḥ yuktaḥ nānā varṇaiḥ haya uttamaiḥ śvetaḥ piśaṅgaḥ sāraṅgaḥ nīlaḥ pītaḥ vilohitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca haritaḥ ca eva pṛṣataḥ pṛśriḥ eva ca daśabhiḥ taiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ akṛśaiḥ vāta raṃhasaiḥ aṣṭa aśvaḥ kāñcanaḥ śrīmān bhaumasya api ratha uttamaḥ tatas ca aṅgirasaḥ vidvān devācāryaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ tatas śanaiścaraḥ api aśvaiḥ sabalaiḥ vyomasaṃbhavaiḥ kārṣṇāyasam samāruhya syandanam yāti vai śanais svarbhānoḥ ca tathā eva aśvāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ hi aṣṭau manojavāḥ ādityāt niḥsṛtaḥ rāhuḥ somam gacchati parvasu atha ketu rathasya aśvāḥ aṣṭau vai vāta raṃhasaḥ palāla dhūma varṇa ābhā sabalāḥ rāsabha aruṇāḥ ete vāhāḥ grahāṇām ca hi upākhyātāḥ rathaiḥ saha vāyavyābhiḥ adṛśyābhiḥ pravṛddhāḥ vāta raśmibhiḥ bhramantam anugacchanti dhruvam te jyotiṣām gaṇāḥ tathā devālayāḥ hi ete ūhyante vāta raśmibhiḥ sarppamāṇāḥ na dṛśyante vyomni deva gaṇāḥ tu te yāvatyaḥ ca eva tārāḥ ca tāvantaḥ vāta raśmayaḥ tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vāta baddhāni sarvaśas sa eṣa tārā mayaḥ jñeyaḥ śiśumāraḥ dhruvaḥ divi yat ahnā kurute pāpam dṛṣṭvā tat niśi muñcate yāvatyaḥ ca eva tārāḥ tāḥ śiśumāra āśritāḥ divi tāvanti eva tu varṣāṇi jīvatā abhyadhikāni tu sākāraḥ śiśumāraḥ ca vijñeyaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ yajñaḥ paraḥ tu vijñeyaḥ dharmaḥ marddhānam āśritaḥ hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ sādhyaḥ hi aśvinau pūrva pādayoḥ varuṇaḥ ca aryamā ca eva paścime tasya sakthinī saṃvatsaraḥ tasya mitraḥ apānam samāśritaḥ pucche agniḥ ca mahendraḥ ca mārīcaḥ kaśyapaḥ dhruvaḥ tārakāḥ śiśumārasya na astam yāti catuṣṭayam nakṣatra candra mūryāḥ ca grahāḥ tārā gaṇaiḥ saha unmukhāḥ vimukhāḥ sarve vakrībhūtāḥ śritāḥ divi dhruveṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ ca eva dhruvam eva pradakṣiṇam pariyānti īśvara śreṣṭham meḍhī bhūtam druvam divi agni indra kaśyapānām tu caramaḥ asau dhruvaḥ smṛtaḥ jyotiṣām cakram etat hi gadā karṣan avāṅmukhaḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahādṛvāyu prokte pūrva bhāge dvitīye anuṣaṅga pāde dhruvacaryākīrttanam nāma trayoviṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca etat śrutvā tu sunayaḥ punar te saṃśaya anvitāḥ yat etat uktam bhavatā gṛhāṇi iti eva vistṛtam katham deva gṛhāṇi syuḥ katham jyotīṃṣi varṇaya etat sarvam samācakṣva jyotiṣām ca eva nirṇayam vāyuḥ uvāca śrutvā tu vacanam teṣām tadā sūtaḥ samāhitaḥ uvāca paramam vākyam teṣām saṃśaya nirṇayam asmin arthe māha aprājñaiḥ yat uktam jñāna buddhibhiḥ yathā deva gṛhāṇi iha sūrya candra grahāḥ smṛtāḥ vyuṣṭāyām tu rajanyām vai brahmaṇaḥ avyakta janmanaḥ avyākṛtam idam tu āsīt naiśena tamasā āvṛtam sarva bhūta avaśiṣṭe asmin loke naṣṭa viśeṣaṇe svayaṃbhūḥ bhagavān tatra loka tantra artha sādhakaḥ saḥ agnim dṛṣṭvā atha loka ādau pṛthivī jala saṃśritam saṃvṛtya tam prakāśa artham tridhā vyamajat īśvaraḥ yaḥ ca asau tapate sūrye śuciḥ agniḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ vaidyutaḥ jāṭharaḥ sauraḥ hi apām garbhāḥ trayaḥ agrayaḥ vaidyutena samāviṣṭaḥ vārṣyaḥ na adbhiḥ praśāmyati mānavāḥ nām ca kukṣi sthaḥ na adbhiḥ śāsyati pāvakaḥ kiñcid apsu matam tejaḥ kiñcid dṛṣṭam abim dhanam kāṣṭha indhanaḥ tu nirmathyaḥ saḥ adbhiḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ arciṣmān pavamānaḥ agniḥ niṣprabhaḥ jāṭharaḥ smṛtaḥ yaḥ ca ayam maṇḍale śuklaḥ nirūṣmā saṃprakāśakaḥ prabhā saurī tu pādena hi astam yāti devākare agnim āviśate rātrau tasmāt dūrāt prakāśate udyantam ca punar sūryam auṣṇa mayam āgneyam āviśat prākāśyam ca tathā auṣṇyam ca saura āgneye tu tejasī uttiṣṭhati punar sūrye rātriḥ āviśate hi apaḥ tasmāt naktam punar śuklāḥ āpaḥ adṛśyanta bhāsvarāḥ pārthiva agni vimiśraḥ asau divyaḥ śuciḥ iti smṛtaḥ ādatte sa tu nāḍīnām sahasreṇa samantataḥ nādeyīḥ ca eva sāmudrīḥ kaupyāḥ ca eva samantataḥ sthāvarāḥ jaṅgamāḥ ca eva yāḥ ca kulyā ādikāḥ apaḥ tasya raśmi sahasram tu śīta varṣa uṣṇa niḥstavam tāsām catuḥśatāḥ nāḍyaḥ varṣante citra mūrttayaḥ candanāḥ ca eva sādhyaḥ ca kūtana akūtanāḥ tathā amṛtāḥ nāmataḥ sarvāḥ raśmayaḥ vṛṣṭi sarjanāḥ hima udgatāḥ ca tābhyaḥ anyāḥ raśmayaḥ tri śatāḥ punar dṛśyāḥ meghāḥ ca yāmyaḥ ca hradinyaḥ hima sarjanāḥ candrāḥ tāḥ nāmataḥ proktāḥ mita ābhāḥ tu gabhastayaḥ śuklāḥ ca kuhakāḥ ca eva gāvaḥ viśva bhṛtaḥ tathā śuklāḥ tāḥ nāmataḥ sarvaḥ triśatāḥ dharma sarjanāḥ samam vibhajya nāḍīḥ tu manuṣṭa pitṛ devatāḥ indraḥ dhātā bhagaḥ pūṣā mitraḥ atha varuṇaḥ ayamā aṃśuḥ vivasvāḥ tvaṣṭā ca savitā viṣṇuḥ eva ca māgha māse tu varuṇaḥ pūṣā ca eva tu phala ālgune caitre māsi tu detoṃśuḥ dhātā vaiśākha tāpanaḥ jyeṣṭha māse bhavet indraḥ ca āṣāḍhe savitā raviḥ vivasvān śrāvaṇe māsi proṣṭhe māse bhāgaḥ smṛtaḥ parjanyaḥ aśvayuje māsi tvaṣṭā ca kārtike raviḥ mārgaśīrṣe bhavet mitraḥ pauṣe viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ pañca raśmi sahasrāṇi varuṇasya arka karmaṇi ṣaḍbhiḥ sahasraiḥ pūṣā tu devaḥ aśu saptabhiḥ tathā dhātā aṣṭabhiḥ sahasraiḥ tu navabhiḥ tu śatakratuḥ savitā daśabhiḥ yāti yāti ekādaśabhiḥ bhagaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ raśmi sahasraiḥ tu viṣaṇuḥ tapati medinīm vasaṃte kapilaḥ sūryaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ śveta varṇaḥ tu varṣāsu pāṇḍuḥ śaradi bhāskaraḥ iti varṇāḥ samā khyātāḥ sūryasya ṛtu samudbhavāḥ auṣadhīṣu balam dhatte svadhayā ca pidṛṣu api bhidyate ṛtum āsādya jala śīta uṣṇa nisravam iti etat maṇḍalam śuklam bhāsvaram sūrya saṃjñitam nakṣatra graha somānām pratiṣṭhā yoniḥ eva ca candra ṛkṣa grahāḥ sarve vijñeyāḥ sūrya saṃbhavāḥ nakṣatra adhipatiḥ somaḥ graha rājaḥ divākaraḥ śeṣāḥ pañca grahāḥ jñeyāḥ īśvarāḥ kāma cāriṇaḥ paṭhyate ca agniḥ ādityaḥ udakam candramāḥ smṛtaḥ śeṣāṇā prakṛtīḥ smayak varṇyamānāḥ nibodhata sura senāpatiḥ skandaḥ paṭhyate aṅgārakaḥ grahaḥ nārāyaṇam budham prāhuḥ veda jñāna vidaḥ budhāḥ mahā grahaḥ dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ manda gāmī śanaiśvaraḥ prajāpati sutau etau ubhau śukra bṛhaspatī āditya mūlam akhilam trailokyam na atra saṃśayaḥ sarva ātmā sarva loka īśaḥ mahādevaḥ prajāpatiḥ bhāva abhāvau hi lokānām ādityāt
